China National Aviation Corporation’s "Kunming" Aircraft: Company Dispatches Personnel for Inspection, Decision on Whether to Transport to Shanghai for Repair Pending Inspection

China National Aviation Corporation's "Kunming" aircraft, flying on the Chongqing-Kunming route, had to make a forced landing at Yizikong, 90 li northeast of Pingyi, on the 5th of this month, while returning from Guiyang to Chongqing, due to sudden and difficult-to-navigate weather. Subsequently, personnel dispatched from both the Guiyang and Kunming stations located the aircraft. Although the aircraft sustained some damage, fortunately, the passengers and flight crew were unharmed. Yesterday morning, a reporter from the New Life News Agency further inquired with the company and learned that all three passengers had already been ordered to be picked up by car at the Kunming station and transferred by plane to Chongqing. As for the aircraft, it is currently still grounded at Yizikong. The company authorities have dispatched mechanical engineers to inspect the extent of the damage to the aircraft and investigate the circumstances of the incident. A decision on whether to transport it to Shanghai for repair will be made after the inspection.

Furthermore, due to the importance of the Chongqing-Kunming route and the critical nature of transportation along that route, the company believes that flights cannot be suspended. However, due to unpredictable weather changes, three engines are necessary to cope with the situation. In addition to planning to dispatch larger aircraft, personnel have been sent to fly to Chongqing to re-inspect the route.

A subcommittee composed of nine banks, including the Bank of Communications, was formed to conduct research. After the subcommittee members convened a meeting, they decided on principles and, after careful research, prepared a report to be submitted to the Association's Executive Committee for review. The Executive Committee reviewed and approved the report and resolved to consult with the finance industry. According to a reporter from the Ta Kung Pao, the Bankers Association has authorized Secretary-General Lin Kanghou to represent the Executive Committee and negotiate with the finance industry on implementation methods. Mr. Lin visited Qin Qiqing, Secretary-General of the Finance Industry Association, to convey the progress of the banking industry's research on the matter and solicit the finance industry's opinions. They had a lengthy and confidential discussion, and progress has been made in the negotiation. Once the authorities of both industries have jointly decided on a unified method, they will submit separate reports to the Ministry of Finance. The report of the banking subcommittee will not be publicly announced until the time is right.

Cotton Control Commission to Expand Seed Distribution Area This Year, Purchasing 21 Tons of American Seeds, to be Transported to Shaanxi, Henan, and Hebei for Distribution

The Cotton Control Commission of the National Economic Council has been working to improve cotton production, and after two years of effort, it has achieved considerable success. As the spring planting season approaches, the Commission has ordered a large quantity of cotton seeds from the United States, preparing to transport them to the Northwest for distribution. This year, the seed distribution area will be expanded to Hebei Province. Details are as follows:

Ordering a Large Quantity of Seeds from the United States

The Cotton Control Commission is working to improve the quality of cotton production in order to have high-quality output. Every year, it orders seeds from the United States and transports them to various improvement areas for distribution and planting. In the past two years, cotton production in the Northwest has gradually achieved considerable success. This year, the Commission has purchased 21 tons of cotton seeds from the United States, which will be transported to various improvement areas and distributed to cotton farmers for planting by the local cotton production improvement institutes.

Expanding Seed Distribution Area to Hebei

In the past, the Commission's cotton improvement work was limited to Shaanxi and Henan provinces. Last year, recognizing that the land in Hebei Province is fertile and very suitable for cotton planting, it planned to distribute seeds in the province. However, the processing time was later, and significant results were not achieved. Therefore, starting this year, the Commission has decided to distribute seeds in Hebei Province, following the same procedures as in Shaanxi and Henan provinces.

Shanghai and Hankou Commodity Inspection Bureaus

Begin Inspecting Asphalt Today

Transfer Zhang Weiru to Serve as Director

According to the China Times News Agency, the Ministry of Industry believes that asphalt is also a major export commodity of China and is closely related to international trade. Cargo Ship Sunk by Tianlun in Xinjiang

Ningbo Native Place Association Cables Ministry for Investigation

After the Incident, Xin Jiangtian Acted as If Nothing Had Happened

Three Drowned in Wanli Boat, No Response to Calls for Help

Also Sends Letters to the Maritime Administration and China Merchants Bureau Requesting Fair Handling

According to the Shanghai Times News Agency, the Ningbo Native Place Association in Shanghai received a letter from the owner of the Jin Wanli sailing boat, reporting that it was sunk by the China Merchants Bureau's Xin Jiangtian steamship. At the time, the crew of the sailing boat called for help, but the steamship ignored them and sped away, resulting in the drowning of three people. The Association has cabled the Ministry of Communications and sent letters to the Maritime Administration and the China Merchants Bureau, requesting a thorough investigation and handling of the matter. The details are recorded below.

Separate Letters to the Two Bureaus

The Ningbo Native Place Association in Shanghai sent separate letters to the Shanghai Maritime Administration and the state-run China Merchants Bureau, requesting a thorough investigation into the sinking of the sailing boat and the drowning of the crew members by the Xin Jiangtian steamship. The original letter stated: "We are writing to inform you that, according to compatriots Wang Youmei and Cao Hongsheng, as well as the bereaved families of the Jin Wanli sailing boat, Youmei and others opened the Tongji Hardware and Oil Company in Ningbo. This time, they purchased 60 tons of diesel oil in Shanghai and entrusted the Gongji Customs Broker to hire the Yu Wanli sailing boat to transport it to Ningbo. Due to waiting for favorable winds, they did not set sail until about 3:00 AM on February 18th. When sailing to the Shuiyawo sandbar in the Sanjia River, they saw a steamship anchored there (the Taigu Company's Chengdu steamship). Our boat sailed six li past that steamship and saw a steamship coming from the opposite direction (namely, the Xin Jiangtian steamship), with a red light hanging on the left side. Our boat immediately sailed to the left, but unexpectedly, the Xin Jiangtian steamship suddenly turned to the left and continued to sail straight ahead, making it impossible to avoid a collision, and our boat was immediately sunk. At the time, the crew members called for help, but the Xin Jiangtian steamship ignored them and sped away. There were a total of eleven crew members on the wooden boat, of whom three drowned and disappeared without a trace. Eight people climbed onto a sampan and drifted with the waves to Wangjiawan in Pudong, where they luckily survived. They immediately reported to the Zhangjiabang Customs. It was not until the 22nd that the details were fully learned. We have reported to the Shanghai Maritime Administration for investigation and have sent a letter to the China Merchants Bureau for negotiation. More than ten days have passed, but we have not received a reply. We have no choice but to appeal to your association to uphold justice and provide assistance." The Association has investigated the case and believes that the sinking of the cargo ship and the drowning of the crew members are extremely serious matters. Based on the above information, we urgently request your bureau to investigate and handle the matter fairly and provide a reply.

Telegram to the Ministry of Communications

The Association also sent a telegram to the Ministry of Communications, requesting it to urgently instruct the Shanghai Maritime Administration to handle the matter fairly. The original telegram stated: "Minister of Communications Yu of Nanjing, according to compatriots Wang Youmei, Cao Hongsheng, and the bereaved families of the Jin Wanli sailing boat (see previous text), more than ten days have passed, but we have not received a reply. Please send a telegram to the Ministry of Communications, instructing the Shanghai Maritime Administration to handle the matter fairly. We are deeply grateful. Ningbo Native Place Association, Yu Qiaqing, etc." The Tax-Paying Chinese Association of the French Concession in Shanghai held a standing committee meeting at 3:00 PM yesterday. Committee members Shang Mujiang, Xu Xiuting, Long Jingyan, Huang Xianggu, Mao Yun, Li Weiliang, and Qu Zhenhua (representing Li Weiliang) attended, and Zhang Shishi was present as an observer. Huang Xianggu chaired the meeting, and Zhang Shishi took the minutes. World-Famous Comedy Star Charlie Chaplin Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday - Actress Paulette Goddard Accompanies Him - Scheduled to Continue South on the Same Ship This Morning

Charlie Chaplin, the world-famous and enduring movie comedy star, decided to travel east with his brother Sydney Chaplin five years ago after completing the film "City Lights." However, because the ship went directly to Hong Kong after passing through Japan, he was unable to visit Shanghai. This time, after completing his new work "Modern Times," he is revisiting the Far East with Paulette Goddard, the rising star actress he discovered (the female lead in "Modern Times"). He arrived in Shanghai yesterday on the Dollar Steamship Company's President Coolidge, after passing through Japan. He is scheduled to continue south on the same ship this morning. His destination is Bali. The details of his arrival and departure are recorded below.

Interview Aboard the Ship - Nearly Escaping in Disguise

The President Coolidge docked at Float No. 12 in the Huangpu River at 1:00 PM yesterday. The passenger ferry departed from the new customs pier at 1:45 PM. No fewer than twenty reporters and photographers from local Chinese and foreign newspapers went to interview and take photos. At around 2:00 PM, although the names of Charlie Chaplin and Paulette Goddard were found on the passenger manifest of the President Coolidge and their first-class cabin FD No. 3 was located, they were nowhere to be seen. Just as people were remembering his escape in disguise from a hotel surrounded by reporters and crowds during his trip to Europe and were afraid that he would repeat his old trick, he was discovered on the deck. Chaplin then became the focus of dozens of cameras, and the sound of "click" was incessant.

Gentlemanly Demeanor - Not Like a Tramp at All

The general impression of Chaplin, whether among men, women, old, young, educated, or uneducated, is that he is like a "tramp," whose staggering and comical walking posture is enough to make people burst into laughter at first sight. However, when he met with reporters, he was a middle-aged gentleman with snow-white hair in his forties. The only resemblance to the Chaplin we see on the screen was his relatively short stature. Miss Goddard was also by his side, leaning on the railing and smiling. The lady is about twenty years old, delicate and lively, like a charming little bird, and is said to be Chaplin's wife.

Waving Goodbye - Revealing a Comical Attitude

When the reporters finished taking photos and were about to ask Chaplin some questions, Chaplin said, "Please meet me at the Cathay Hotel at 6:30 PM tonight, and we can talk freely." He then went down the President Coolidge with Miss Goddard and others and boarded the specially prepared "Gypsy" yacht, which first met the passenger ship and sailed upstream, cutting through the waves. After boarding the yacht, he seemed uneasy that the reporters were left on the passenger ferry, so he waved goodbye through the window, unintentionally revealing his comical posture, which made everyone laugh. In fact, the reason why Chaplin has achieved today's position is precisely because he often reveals such sincere emotions in every film he stars in.

Impression of Shanghai - Just One Sentence: Too Exciting

At 6:30 PM, the reporters gathered again. After Chaplin disembarked, he was invited by friends to tour the city for a preliminary sightseeing. They were led to the A-shaped room on the fifth floor. The room's layout and furnishings were purely British style, as a gift from the Cathay Hotel management, perhaps because Chaplin is British. Miss Goddard stayed in Room No. 9 on the same floor, opposite Chaplin's room. After Chaplin entered the room, he lit a cigarette and sat by the fireplace. Regarding his first impression of Shanghai, he said, "Too exciting."

Marriage Question - A Wonderful Evasive Answer

He then said that this trip started from Hollywood in the film city, passing through Honolulu, Japan, and Shanghai. He will take the original ship to Hong Kong tomorrow morning and then go to Manila, Bali, Indochina, and other places. The entire trip will be completed in May. He may come to Shanghai again for a short stay in March. Chaplin is the only opponent of sound films, only advocating dubbing to enhance the drama of the play. "City Lights" is his successful attempt. He has not wavered in this view to this day. He believes that sound films create obstacles to acting everywhere. Therefore, in "Modern Times," he still did not speak, only sang. When reporters asked if he had been engaged to or married Miss Goddard, he smiled and said that this question should be answered by Miss Goddard, which can be described as a wonderful evasion. He currently has no plans to continue starring in films but intends to direct a film starring Miss Goddard. It is rumored that he intends to shoot a film in Bali, which is impossible because he has not brought any filming equipment. Regarding the Far East issue, he said that when he was in Japan, people also asked for his thoughts, but he did not say much.

Starring in Various Films - Earning General Sympathy

Chaplin has been making comedy films in the United States for twenty-two years. He writes, directs, and stars in all of them. He is not only a skilled film actor but also a philosopher of life, a sociologist, and an artist, and is loved by film audiences all over the world. The films he stars in are often satirical and sympathetic to the general public.

Two Gunny Sacks - Containing Eight Pieces of a Dissected Corpse - Strange Murder Case - Truth Still Unknown

A strange murder case was discovered at 6:00 AM yesterday in the small river in the western part of Kangqu Bridge, Kangqu Road, Nanshi. Zhou Chen, a woman living at No. 1397 Kangqu Road, saw a man picking up trash in the small river while she was out washing clothes. He used a bamboo hook to pull two gunny sacks to the riverbank. Upon inspecting the sacks, she found eight horrifying pieces of a male corpse. The head and body were divided into two sections and placed in one gunny sack. The arms were divided into two sections, and the legs and feet were divided into four sections and placed in another sack. The deceased was estimated to be in his thirties or forties. It appeared that he was murdered and then dissected into eight pieces to move the body and escape punishment. The corpse's face had no fresh blood and the skin appeared purple and yellow. The woman reported the incident to the police station, who in turn ordered the local police chief to report to the court for an autopsy. In the afternoon at 4:00 PM yesterday, Prosecutor Li was assigned to lead the coroner and others to the scene. The autopsy revealed that the deceased had indeed been murdered before being dissected and moved here. It was ordered that the death certificate be filled out and photos taken, and that the body be placed in a coffin by the charitable organization and the murderer be arrested and investigated.

Qingpu Kidnapping Case: Bandits Captured in Shanghai, Two Victims, Zhusheng and Rongsheng, Rescued; Court Approves Transfer to Qingpu for Trial

Around midnight on December 19th of last year, a group of bandits suddenly appeared at the home of wealthy Zhang Guixing in Jiagang Village, Qianta Township, thirty miles southwest of Qingpu County. They kidnapped Zhang's grandson, Ah Hugen (four years old). Upon hearing the alarm, the local militia rushed to apprehend them. The bandits opened fire, killing militiaman Gu Shaolin. The bandits then fled with the victim, demanding a ransom of 30,000 yuan. Zhao Zhen, a detective from the Second Team of the First District of the Jiangsu Provincial River Security Force, learned that the kidnappers were hiding in Shanghai. He came to Shanghai with an official letter and, around 10 PM the other night, collaborated with Pang Yutang, a Chinese detective of the Old Zha police station. They rushed to the Yong'an Company's amusement park and arrested Zhu Ziliang (also known as Songliang), a native of Pudong, who was involved in the case. Subsequently, at No. 47 Li Mei Road in the French Concession, they apprehended two more accomplices, Wu A'jin (also known as Jinsheng), a native of Pudong, and his concubine, Chen Fengbao. They also rescued two young kidnap victims, Li Zhusheng (13 years old) and Li Rongsheng (9 years old), who had been kidnapped from Nanbang, Qingpu. Zhusheng's father is named Yutang, and Rongsheng's father is named Qingtang. All were taken back to the police station. Later, Wei Shixiong was apprehended at No. 44 Luzon Road. Yesterday morning, they were all taken to the First Special District Court's Criminal Court No. 1. Wang Yaotang, the police station's lawyer, explained the situation and agreed to the Qingpu River Public Security Team's request for transfer. Zhao Zhen then filed the case, requesting approval for the transfer. He stated that the victim, Ah Hugen, had not yet been rescued, and the official letter would be submitted later due to time constraints. When questioned, all defendants confessed. Judge Feng reviewed the confessions and ordered the four defendants and the two rescued victims to be handed over to the Qingpu officials for investigation.

French Concession: Red Pill Manufacturing Den Cracked; Two Siblings, the Masterminds, Flee; Two Women Arrested for Interrogation

Lu Zhulin, a detective, and Song Yunfeng, a constable of the French Police, learned on the 7th of this month that someone was privately manufacturing red pills at No. 32, Bing'an Lane, Ailai Ge Road. They immediately reported to West Inspector Bu Xiaokao, and together they went to the location. They arrested Wang Nannan, an 18-year-old woman from Changshu, and Chen Sanyuan, a 23-year-old woman. They seized 4,000 red pills. The women confessed that the owners were Zhang Genlin and Zhang Qiaolin, siblings, but their current whereabouts are unknown. They also confessed that other dens were located at No. 11 Hengmao Lane, Tiniyin Road, and No. 10 Zhengjia Muqiao. Upon receiving this information, the detectives immediately searched those two locations. They seized 6,000 red pills in the attic of No. 10 Zhonghua Lane, and a large quantity of equipment for manufacturing red pills, such as drying boxes, was seized at No. 11 Hengmao Lane. However, no one was apprehended at either location. They were taken to the police station and sent to the Second Special District Court's Criminal Court yesterday afternoon. The police station's lawyer first explained the case and requested an extension to investigate further. When questioned, Wang Nannan confessed that she was a maid in Bing'an Lane and knew nothing about the red pill manufacturing. Chen Sanyuan claimed that she was visiting Wang Nannan in Bing'an Lane and was mistakenly arrested. Their other statements were evasive. Judge Li ordered a further hearing on the morning of the 19th.

Hengxiang Bank Opium Case: Tea Boy Testifies; Defendant Shao Liangru Denies; Xu and Yue Each Post 1,000 Yuan Bail

Due to the discovery of a large amount of opium at the Hengxiang Bank, located at No. 18, Lane 120, Ningbo Road, Song Bingzheng, a Chinese detective chief, and Liu Junjie and Bao Lisheng, detectives of the Chief Inspectorate, went to search the premises. They seized over a hundred taels of opium and paraphernalia and arrested Shao Liangru (also known as Jian San), the bank's manager, and Xu Shixian (also known as Yansheng) and Yue Xiubiao (also known as Ming San). The First Special District Court interrogated them and adjourned the case. Shao was later released on bail by the court. Yesterday morning, Judge Feng Shide reopened the Criminal Court No. 1 for further interrogation. Wang Yaotang, the police station's lawyer, stated that the police had found a former tea boy at the bank named Zhou A'jin, who testified that on January 24th of this year, the defendant Shao Liangru ordered him and the driver Hai Sheng to move two wooden boxes into the vault. Shao then opened the boxes, which were full of opium. The next day, Shao ordered people to smoke opium for a whole day and then repackaged it into cigarette tins, which Hai Sheng transported out in batches. He also saw Shao's friend and an unknown man come to collect several packages of opium. He wrote a statement. However, Zhou was not present today, and the police still need to continue their investigation, so they requested an adjournment. When questioned, Shao Liangru denied these facts, claiming that there was no tea boy named Zhou A'jin in his employment. The driver, Zhang Haisheng, also testified that he did not know Zhou A'jin and that the facts were not as Zhou stated. The defendants' lawyers, Fan Gang, E'sen, and Wu Lin Kun, objected to the police's request, stating that the medical examiner had found that the defendants Xu Shixian and Yue Xiubiao were not opium addicts and requested that they be released on bail. Judge Feng adjourned the case. Xu and Yue each posted a bail of 1,000 yuan.

Gu Zhuxuan Case: Public Trial Today; Ma Brothers Still at Large

Gu Zhuxuan, a key suspect in the incitement of the assassination of Tang Jiapeng, allegedly incited false testimony while detained at the external hospital (i.e., Guangci Police Hospital). The Second Special District Court's Procuratorate repeatedly interrogated the case. As a result, Gu Zhuxuan's brother, Gu Songmao, and guards Wu Jing, Ma Xianxiang, and the two escaped Ma brothers and Wang Yushou were all suspected of inciting perjury. A public prosecution was filed with the Criminal Court of the same court. The Ma brothers had previously submitted statements to both courts, and the Procuratorate had ordered them to appear for questioning, but they had not turned themselves in after many days. It is now learned that the case is scheduled for a public trial at 2:00 PM today by Judge Li Changnian in Criminal Court No. 1.

Adulterer and Adulteress Caught in Bed; Husband's Jealousy Leads to Stabbing; Wife Injured, Man Arrested

Man Zhengzhen, a 36-year-old native of Zhenjiang, lived in a lean-to at No. 11 Maidie'an Road in the French Concession. He used to work as a clerk at the Huaqing Bathhouse on Sanma Road but had been unemployed for the past month. Man's wife, Tan, 28, had been unfaithful and recently became involved with Fu Laoda, a Jurong native who worked as a back scrubber in the Chunquan Port area of Zhabei. The other night, while her husband was out, Tan invited Fu Laoda to her home for a tryst. Just as Man Zhengzhen returned home and pushed open the door, he saw the adulterer and adulteress sleeping in bed together. Consumed by jealousy, he grabbed an iron ladle and struck his wife Tan on the head. Seeing the situation, the adulterer fled. At that moment, Tan also became enraged and grabbed a kitchen knife to attack her husband. Man Zhengzhen stepped forward and disarmed her. Tan's right middle and index fingers were severed by the knife, and Man struck Tan on the head with the knife, causing her to bleed profusely. Huang A'er and others, who lived nearby, heard the commotion and rushed in, horrified. They reported the incident to the police station, who ordered officers to arrest Man and take the murder weapon to the police station. The injured woman was taken to the hospital. Yesterday afternoon, Man was taken to the Second Special District Court's Criminal Court No. 1. The police station's lawyer first described the case and requested a postponement. When questioned, Man Zhengzhen stated that his wife was having an affair, which he already knew. Because he had no proof, he did not take action. Yesterday afternoon around 3:00 PM, his wife gave him three yuan and told him to return to his hometown to find work. He knew it was a ploy to get him out of the house, so he pretended to agree and secretly went to chat with friends. When he returned home at 11:30 PM and pushed open the door, he found the adulterer and adulteress in bed together, so he committed the act. Judge Li ordered a further hearing on the 19th. The defendant was remanded in custody.

Xue Wencuan, a 67-year-old local resident of No. 17 Xinzha Road in the Public Concession, was old and frail. The other night, he attended a wedding banquet at a relative's home in West Shanghai. Xue, drunk and unsteady, fell into the creek and drowned. Foreign Boy Killed in Bike Accident

Berser, a 17-year-old Dutch national residing at No. 1331, Lafayette Road, and his friends, John van Sinter (a 15-year-old Dutch national) and Ainidu Berser (an 18-year-old Russian national), were riding bicycles, planning to go to the Hongqiao Garden the other morning around 11:00 AM. Establishment of China Textile World Society

Textile expert Wang Yiming has held important positions in major yarn mills in the country for nearly two decades. Since resigning as engineer of the Hubei Shashi Yarn Mill last year, he has witnessed the decline of China's textile industry and has united with colleagues in the domestic textile industry to form the China Textile World Society and publish the "Textile World Weekly" to study the reasons for the decline of the textile industry and the improvement of technology. He has received the support of leaders in the textile industry and is actively preparing for publication within the month. The society is located at No. 5 Chongrang Lane, Fuzhou Road, Shanghai, telephone 92005.

Wang Changlin's Stepmother Wu Shi's Appeal Case Concludes Yesterday; Years of Nurturing Meant to Obtain Filial Piety; Failure to Provide Support Violates Law and Humanity

Wang Shi, the stepmother of Wang Changlin, a manager at the Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank, is 64 years old. Because her son did not support her after returning from studying abroad, and after repeated arguments, he only gave her 40 yuan per month, which was not enough to live on, she filed a lawsuit against Changlin last winter, demanding support and repayment of educational expenses. The First Special District Court made a preliminary judgment. However, Wang Shi, believing that the judgment was not in line with her request, hired a lawyer to appeal to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. Wang Changlin also expressed dissatisfaction with the original judgment and filed a counterclaim. Yesterday afternoon, the judges of the Second Branch of the High Court held a joint trial. Neither party was present in person, and each was represented by a lawyer. First, Wang Shi's lawyer stated the grounds for the appeal, stating that what the appellant requested in the first instance was to: 1. Repay various debts incurred since 19 years ago, totaling 5,000 yuan; 2. Pay 100 yuan per month for alimony from November of last year. The preliminary judgment ordered Wang Changlin to repay 1,300 yuan for the first item and to pay 60 yuan per month for the second item, which was too far apart from what was requested. That is why the appeal was filed. Changlin was adopted by Wang Shi as her successor at the age of 14. The latter spared no expense to educate him. He went abroad to study at the age of 22. During these years, most of the family property that was sold was used to nurture Changlin, hoping that he would be able to fulfill his filial duty in the future. However, when he returned to the country in 18 years, he drove his stepmother away in 19 years. Later, although he gave 40 yuan per month for alimony, it was rarely given willingly and only given sporadically after repeated requests, causing the woman to live in debt. Over the years, including medical expenses, she has spent over 10,000 yuan. Now she is only asking for 5,000 yuan, which is the lowest amount. Changlin currently lives in a Western-style house and drives a car, and owns land in Jiangwan and other places. His life is prosperous and luxurious, which is due to his higher education. However, the one who educated him is now suffering. From the perspective of law and humanity, Changlin should not be so abusive. However, at the first hearing of the first instance, he denied that the woman was his stepmother and then threatened to litigate to the end. The woman is in her twilight years and cannot bear this. Moreover, creditors are constantly knocking on the door, and her livelihood is difficult. She should be judged according to the amount requested by the woman and the appeal of the respondent should be rejected. Then, Wang Changlin's lawyer argued that Shi left home on her own initiative under the pretext of going to Hangzhou to burn incense. How could she be accused of being driven away? And since August of 19 years, he has been giving 40 yuan per month, and he has not heard any objections. The woman originally owned hundreds of thousands of dollars of family property, which she sold over the years, and Changlin never touched a penny. Her intention to increase the alimony is because Changlin only earned 180 yuan when he paid 40 yuan, and now he earns more than 300 yuan a month, so she also wants to increase it. In fact, Changlin's current financial situation is far from what it used to be. Therefore, he requested that the original judgment be reversed and that 40 yuan be given per month and the appellant's appeal be rejected. Judge Han then declared the debate closed and scheduled the judgment for a later date.

Seventh Group Wedding: List Announced Yesterday; One Hundred Couples Approved to Participate; Wedding Ceremony to Be Held on April 1st

The group wedding pioneered by the city's Social Affairs Bureau has been held for a year since the first ceremony was held in April last year. Six ceremonies have been held, with over 600 couples participating. Provinces and cities have followed suit, and the trend of frugal weddings has spread throughout the country. Prefectures in Japan have also imitated it and have achieved good results. The seventh group wedding ceremony will be held on April 1st. Since registration began on February 10th, it has been full in less than ten days. Over 70 couples were turned away due to being full. Its enthusiasm is unprecedented. In order to maintain order in the hall, the Social Affairs Bureau had to set a limit of 100 couples. According to the person in charge of the bureau, the bureau deeply regrets those who could not participate due to being full. In the future, it will plan remedial measures within the possible scope. The details are divided below:

Ceremony Date

The seventh group wedding ceremony will be held at 3:00 PM on April 1st in the city government auditorium. All applicants have been investigated and 100 couples have been approved to participate. The married couple should wear the prescribed dress and pants of the same color as the dress. The groom should wear white socks and black satin shoes with pink soles. No gloves are required. The bride should wear shoes and socks of the same color as the dress, wear long gloves, and hold a bouquet of flowers. No difference is allowed.

Stamping Practice

Those approved to marry should go to the Social Affairs Bureau with the officiant to stamp and receive the registration certificate. The stamping dates are as follows: No. 1 to No. 25, March 25th morning; No. 26 to No. 50, 25th afternoon; No. 51 to No. 75, 26th morning; No. 76 to No. 100, 26th afternoon. All married people should participate in the wedding ceremony practice at 2:00 PM on March 31st. The Social Affairs Bureau will provide large cars for transportation.

Origin Statistics

The origin of the married people participating in the seventh group wedding includes 46 men from Zhejiang, 36 from Jiangsu, 6 from Guangdong, 4 from Shanghai, 2 from Anhui, 2 from Hubei, 1 from Hunan, 1 from Jiangxi, 1 from Henan, and 1 from Jilin; 40 women from Jiangsu, 39 from Zhejiang, 10 from Guangdong, 6 from Shanghai, 2 from Anhui, 1 from Hubei, 1 from Hebei, and 1 from Jiangxi. The age of the married people is the highest for men at 24 years old, the youngest is 18 years old, and the oldest is 41 years old. For women, the age of the married people is the highest at 20 years old, the oldest is 29 years old, and the youngest is 16 years old. In terms of occupation, the most men are company employees, accounting for 49%. In addition, all walks of life are represented, and only one is unemployed. 73% of women are engaged in housework. In addition, middle school students and elementary school teachers are the most common. There are also three female workers.

Eighth Registration

The eighth group wedding ceremony will be held on June 3rd. Registration will begin on April 10th and end on the 30th. The limit is still 100 couples. In view of the previous enthusiasm, those who wish to participate should apply as early as possible.

Rickshaw Pullers Mutual Aid Association - Medical Care for Rickshaw Pullers' Illnesses

The Shanghai Rickshaw Pullers Mutual Aid Association recognized the extreme need of its members for medical assistance. Therefore, from its inception, it established clinics, employing well-known Chinese and Western doctors dedicated to social service to provide treatment. Currently, the five clinics have a total of more than twenty doctors and nurses. From November 10, 1934, to the end of February 1936, the total number of visits by members and their families to the clinics for Chinese and Western medical treatment reached 11,131 times. If a member is unable to pull a rickshaw due to illness, the association provides rice as assistance. For serious illnesses beyond the capabilities of the clinics, patients are sent to hospitals for treatment, with medical expenses and accommodation costs paid by the association. This has benefited over a hundred people. The association has also decided to establish its own sanatorium, located above the branch association in the western district, which will soon be completed and opened. The internal facilities include more than twenty beds, a pathology laboratory, a surgical operating room, a patient bathroom, sterilization and washing facilities, and all food and drink for inpatients are provided by the sanatorium. Furthermore, for those who are too sick to visit the clinics, in addition to the association's doctors providing house calls, health counselors visit their homes daily for巡迴看護（nursing rounds）. The number of people receiving this nursing care has reached 6,459. This demonstrates the association's attention to the health of rickshaw pullers and the true value of their work.

First Dairy Cattle Competition - Regulations for the Competition - A Total of Five Groups Participating - Soliciting Prizes for the Winners

The first dairy cattle competition organized by the Municipal Livestock Improvement Promotion Association has been scheduled for April 26 at the Jiangwan Racecourse. Regarding the competition regulations, our reporter from the Datong News Agency has learned the following:

Contest Location: Mu City Jiangwan Racecourse

Date: April 26, 1936

Participating Cattle: Dairy bulls or cows within the city limits that have passed the veterinary examination by the association may participate.

Categories of Cattle: The cattle will be divided into five groups based on their breed, body type, and coat color: A. Local Improved Cattle Group; B. Guernsey Cattle Group; C. Holstein Cattle Group; D. Ayrshire Cattle Group; E. Alderney Cattle Group.

Cattle Judging: The association will invite several livestock experts and dairy industry leaders to form a judging committee to follow the latest judging standards from around the world.

Source of Prizes: The association will solicit prizes from party and government agencies, academic groups, industrial magnates, and other enthusiastic individuals.

Child Abduction - Monk Ni Arrested the Other Day

Gen Sheng, the five-year-old boy of Wang Liu, a woman from Tongzhou who previously lived at No. De'anli, Taopeng Road, disappeared while playing at the door at 3:00 PM on November 10 last year. There has been no news of him since. Recently, a fellow villager, Monk Ni, went to Ms. Wang's home at No. 2 Linqing Road and said, "Your child was abducted by Ni Futang. He can be found, but it will cost 40 yuan." Ms. Wang knew that he was the mastermind, so she feigned agreement to raise the money and secretly followed him to Guianli, Linyin Road, Nanshi, where she saw him enter. The next day, she inquired and Futang claimed that he had abducted the child at the time and temporarily placed him with Yu in Pudong. He has now taken him to his home in Nantong and hidden him. Ms. Wang immediately returned to the village and reported to the Yulin Road Police Station, which dispatched Detective Li Hongsheng to secretly go with detectives from the Public Security Bureau to arrest Monk Ni the other day. He was taken back to the police station and detained. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Third Criminal Court of the Special First Court. Lawyer Zhang Shizhu from the Engineering Bureau recounted the case and said that the defendant claimed at the police station that Ms. Wang had been living with him for many years and that the child was born to Ms. Wang's former husband. The child is currently in Zhang Xingzhen, Lao Honggang, Nantong, at his father's place. Ms. Wang went there to negotiate with him, but the father, Lao Ni, said that he had spent 28 yuan to buy the child. Later, they went together to the local Public Security Bureau to temporarily detain Wang's child. Ms. Wang has not yet appeared in court, so please postpone the case and send an official letter from the court to the Nantong County Government to bring the child to Shanghai. The defendant was questioned, and his statements were evasive. Judge Jiang Shuzi ordered him to be remanded in custody and rescheduled the case for further investigation.

Two Cases of Assaults for Debt Collection

At the intersection of Guangdong Road and Jingyuan Street, Guangdong Road, at around 8:00 PM last night, a rogue named Long Huaqing, 26 years old, was demanding a debt of 3 yuan from another rogue surnamed Zhang. However, Mr. Zhang had no money on him, which led to an argument. Long Huaqing grabbed him and refused to let go, threatening violence. Unexpectedly, Mr. Zhang pulled out a sharp knife and stabbed Long Huaqing in the chest, deeply injuring his lung. Long Huaqing, in great pain, immediately released his grip and fell to the ground, bleeding profusely. The assailant took the opportunity to escape. Nearby constables heard the alarm and arrived, taking him to the hospital for treatment, where his condition was critical.

Xinzha Road A Jiangbei man named Zhao Guibao, 26 years old, had a big dispute with a man named Yang Dabai on the roadside at around 2:00 PM yesterday afternoon while passing through Xinzha Road. It is reported that Zhao Guibao owed Li Dabai 12 yuan in hui money and had not returned it for a long time. Therefore, when Li encountered Zhao Guibao, he demanded it from him, which led to the dispute. However, Zhao Guibao stubbornly refused to pay. Li Dabai became impatient and pulled out a hidden knife, stabbing Zhao in the left shoulder before fleeing. Zhao screamed for help. Nearby constables heard the news and rushed to the scene, but the assailant had already fled. They quickly took him to the hospital for treatment and reported the case to the police station.

Theft - Case Solved for Traffic Cargo

Recently, thefts of passenger and freight have occurred at the Shanghai North Railway Station Qiujiang Road Joint Transportation Freight Depot, and thieves have impersonated employees of specialized transportation companies to design fraud to transport goods. The relevant Su-Song Third Police Section, after receiving reports, secretly ordered an investigation and has solved the entire case. The detailed process is as follows:

Cargo Fraud

Wang Er, a 26-year-old man from Shangyu, Zhejiang, is idle and does not engage in honest work. However, he is well-dressed, and at first glance, he looks like a formal businessman. Unexpectedly, he is full of tricks and mixed into the North-South Joint Transportation Freight Depot, impersonating an employee of the local Huashengyi Transportation Company, stealing a bundle of North-South Joint Transportation cargo labels and taking the opportunity to defraud. On the 4th of this month, Zeng Yiji Tobacco Shop at No. 29, Kai Feng Road, Re He Road, sent a clerk, Zhu Ruilian, pushing a rickshaw, to deliver several pieces of passenger and freight (said to be porcelain clocks, thermos bottles, and other foreign sundries) to the North Station for transportation. Wang found out about this and used all kinds of tricks to deceive her and took the goods. When the fraud was discovered and reported to the police, Wang had already taken the stolen goods and fled with his accomplices.

Investigation and Arrest

Unexpectedly, after a few days, Wang had spent all the money he had obtained from selling the stolen goods. He was again tempted to commit crimes and secretly returned to the original place, intending to use the same tricks. However, Zhu Ruilian was investigating after being deceived. They met face to face, and Zhu immediately grabbed him and handed him over to the traffic police for investigation. Wang initially denied it, but with Zhu's accurate identification, he could not deny it. He then claimed that he had accomplices who were hiding in the French Concession. As a result, the investigation was unsuccessful. Later, Chen Shenggong, an employee of Wang Hongji Transportation Company at No. 5, Baoshanli, Qipanjie, Wuma Road, brought a witness, Chuan Xiangsheng, to the traffic police station to accuse Zhu of stealing a large hemp bag of tin foil worth 150 yuan from the company on the 28th of last month and requested a joint investigation.

Referral to the Court

The traffic police section believed that Wang dared to steal railway joint transportation labels and repeatedly defrauded and stole goods from merchants, seriously disrupting business. Furthermore, after investigating, they found that he had committed the crime with accomplices and that there might be more than two cases. After detailed investigation for several days, Wang still tried to reduce his crime, claiming that he was not the main offender. However, all the plaintiffs identified him without error. Yesterday morning (9th), the section recorded the statements of all parties and sent them, along with the evidence found, to the Shanghai District Court for strict punishment. It is also reported that the goods that Wang defrauded and stole from various companies were stolen in transit on Qiujiang Road and were not goods that the railways had already received, so the railway bureau had no responsibility. Therefore, various companies dare not be careless in handling transportation procedures in the future.

Zhili Plums to be Publicly Distributed

Zhili plums are of excellent quality and taste the best among all fruits. They are produced in Tongxiang, Zhejiang, and have a long-standing reputation. Those who get them cherish them, because the cultivators are generally old farmers, resulting in a feudal nature and unwillingness to spread them to the outside world. Therefore, those who seek them out of admiration have often been met with cold shoulders. Mr. Gao from the Central Agricultural Experiment Station is extremely concerned about fruit tree horticulture, so he has collected a rich collection of good varieties from China and abroad, and he has always regretted not having Zhili plums. Later, through the introduction of a friend, he met the owner of a Zhili plum garden in that area and spent several years of hard work to obtain true variety grafting buds. He uses the latest scientific methods to engage in propagation and has established a general office at Ermuyuan, Fulili Road, Shanghai, and branch offices at Liuhe Lane, Minquan Road, Liuduqiao, Hankou, to prepare for the public distribution of all the seedlings raised this autumn. Since this news spread, those who know about it have been rushing to place orders with the experimental station.

Report of the Guangdong-Guangxi Industrial Inspection Group

— Respectfully

Organization and Career of Industrial Mission Members

The Guangdong-Guangxi Industrial Inspection Group was sponsored by the China General Confederation of Industry and Commerce. Mr. Wang Zhisheng first made contact in advance and was welcomed by the authorities and local people of Guangdong and Guangxi. The purpose of this trip was to inspect the industry in Guangdong and Guangxi, and to exchange opinions with the industrial circles and authorities of the two provinces in order to achieve mutual cooperation in industry. A total of 36 members joined the group. Mr. Cai Shengbai was elected as the head of the group, and Mr. Xiang Kangyuan and Mr. Hu Xiyuan were his deputies. Before leaving, Mr. Yang Dezhao, the Guangdong provincial representative stationed in Shanghai, hosted a dinner. The reporter talked about the industrial and commercial situation in Guangdong Province. Mr. Yang was very clear. He first said that the silk-producing areas in Guangdong are mainly in Shunde, Nanhai, Zhongshan, and Panyu. Shunde's silkworm cocoons are said to be well-developed, but recently, due to the low price of silk and the influx of foreign goods and rayon, they have been lagging behind. The annual value has fallen from 90 million yuan to several million yuan. The provincial government recognizes the silk industry as one of the province's sources of wealth, so it is doing its best to promote it. The improved breeding grounds have been reduced to ten, and a special bureau has been established to take charge of it. At present, the cost of improving each breeding card is three yuan, but it is only sold to silkworm farmers for one yuan. Academic institutions, such as Zhongda Lingnan and Zhongkai, are all studying the silk industry. Shunde has always been a very promising area for agriculture. Farmers enjoy the pleasure of family wealth by raising fish and pigs, planting mulberry trees, and raising silkworms. Therefore, there is a custom of women not marrying. However, recently, a large number of sweet potatoes, pigs, and cattle from Taiwan have been imported at very low prices. The price of cattle is only more than ten yuan per head, and sweet potatoes only cost five jiao per box (transportation box, the price of each pair is two jiao and five fen), which is very worrying. The sugar industry, in terms of raw materials, is not only encouraging sugarcane farmers to grow sugarcane widely and borrowing money from the Shanghai financial industry, but the provincial government has now established six sugar factories, all of which are very large in scale. In the future, with the completion of the Yuehan Railway and the completion of the Huangpu Commercial Port, the industry in Guangdong Province will have more room for development. The Guangdong Provincial Three-Year Economic Construction Plan will be completed soon. The future plan has been slightly changed. Heavy industry is of course run by the province itself, and light industry will be opened up as much as possible and operated by merchants. The government also intends to implement interest protection and provide loans. At the same time, plans for the propagation and preservation of fruits are also underway, hoping to spread from one province to the whole country, etc. Mr. Yang travels between Shanghai and Guangdong and has extraordinary insights and experience. I greatly admire him. Then, we talked about the currency and tax system issues. Mr. Yang said that it is a pity that the currency system in Guangdong Province has not yet been unified, but this kind of problem seems to be a national issue. There are also various reasons for the collection of taxes. I hope that after arriving in Guangdong, we can earnestly negotiate with each other and there is no worry that there will be no solution. On the evening of the 3rd, all the members of the delegation set off on the President Jefferson. The reporter counted the careers of the 36 members of the delegation as follows: six in the chemical industry, four in the dyeing and weaving industry, three in the electrical appliance industry, two in the machinery industry, two in the enamel industry, two in the pharmaceutical industry, one in the textile industry, one in the silk weaving industry, one in the tobacco industry, one in the bakelite industry, one in the knitting industry, one in the flour industry, one in the rubber industry, one in the cement industry, one in the glue industry, one in the refrigeration industry, one in the paint industry, one in the canning industry, one in the condiment industry, one in the transportation industry, one in the printing industry, and two representatives of national goods groups.

A total of 22 industries, with the chemical industry being the most numerous. Chemists Wu Yun Chu. Fang Yexian and Wu Qingtai all joined the trip. The gathering of talents opened a new era for the Bao Industrial Inspection Group. The members of the ship gathered and made two resolutions. What was discussed was the inspection schedule and the points to pay attention to when visiting, and the grouping inspection was based on their own expertise, which was valuable.

Sports News

The Upcoming International Games May Be Postponed Due to Date Conflicts with the National Team's Overseas Trip

As the weather warms and the track and field season approaches, the annual Shanghai International Track and Field Games, as usual, should be held in May. According to Shen Siliang of the Physical Education Association, this year's international games may be difficult to hold due to a date conflict with the departure of our country's Olympic team. There will likely be little time to hold a competition with Western expatriates before their departure. If the games are held after the team returns from Germany, it may be too cold for track and field competitions. Therefore, this year's international track and field games may be postponed. In any case, a decision must wait until the team returns to Shanghai from Beiping (Beijing) and Tianjin.

Junior Cup

This season's Junior Cup also had 26 teams competing. In the third week, Yu You eliminated Tung Wah 3-2, while St. Francis eliminated Qinghua 10-0. Subsequently, the British Navy team returned home, and Lancashire took over their spot. By the fourth week of quarterfinals, Weisheng and St. Francis were eliminated by Lancashire and Yu You, respectively, earning the right to the final. Lancashire has an impressive record in Hong Kong and has repeatedly demonstrated its skills since arriving in Shanghai. The clash of these two strong teams in the final promises a fierce battle. However, Yu You recently defeated Lancashire 1-0 in the quarterfinals of the North China Daily News Cup. Based on this, Yu You has high hopes for the trophy. The Junior Cup results are as follows: (Yu You and Lancashire are scheduled for the final this Saturday.) (Note) Lancashire defeated Weisheng 5-2 in the quarterfinals, earning the right to the final.

Duisburg, Germany, March 9th (Reuters): Danish swimmer Johnson recently completed the 400-meter breaststroke in 5 minutes and 4.5 seconds, breaking the world record. (Note: The original world record was 5 minutes and 5.2 seconds, set by German swimmer Rademacher on March 6, 1926.)

After Mayor Wu of this city initiated a citywide public small-soccer competition and entrusted the Shanghai Small Soccer Association to handle it, the association has been actively proceeding to launch the competition within a month. The association's preparations are outlined below:

Meeting of Cadres: The association was originally organized to participate in the small-soccer performance at the 6th National Games. Participation Method: The association has learned from the malpractices of previous competitions. Therefore, this time, the participation method will be resolutely reformed. In addition to a small registration fee, no security deposit will be collected from the registered teams. However, those who forfeit once will be disqualified from the competition. The handling will be earnest in order to uphold sportsmanship and serve as an example for the sports community.

The Shandong University Incident Expands: The Public Security Bureau Arrests More Than 30 Students; The School Dismisses Another 13 Students

Qingdao News: After He Siyuan, Director of the Shandong Education Department, arrived in Qingdao on the evening of the 6th, he summoned the students on the 7th to give a speech, urging them to resume classes as soon as possible. This morning (the 8th), the police surrounded Shandong University and arrested 31 students (including 8 female students). Shanghai Completes a Children's Film Network; Eight Branches Established Simultaneously Today; Children's Films Screened Every Sunday

The Shanghai Children's Welfare Committee, recognizing the importance of film in children's education, established a Children's Film Promotion Committee to handle this matter. Children's films have been shown every Sunday morning. To expand the promotion, the committee convened a conversation meeting with the principals of various elementary schools last week to discuss solutions. It was decided to establish branches and nominate Xu Gongmei and Sun Yongyi as committee members to draft regulations and be responsible for establishing the branches. It is understood that the branches are ready. Eight branches will be established in various districts of Shanghai, centered on the Southeast, Rongjin, Xihai, Donghai, Shijie, Shanxi, Jincheng, and Paris cinemas. Nearby elementary schools can become members of the branches. The eight branches established today will hold their founding meetings at 3:00 PM in each cinema. Representatives from the headquarters will provide guidance. In addition to selecting and introducing films suitable for children, the member schools will also assign teachers to conduct civic training and impart general knowledge to the children before the screenings so that children can obtain beneficial guidance at any time to supplement the deficiencies of school education. In the future, a dense network of children's films will be established throughout the city, which will have considerable benefits for children's education.

Matters Needing Attention for Children's Films:

All films shown in each session should be suitable for children and decided by the branches.

The cinema should mark "Children's Film Day" in front of the cinema during the screening and add special decorations.

Each cinema should send explanatory brochures, advertisements, and preferential tickets to each member school in advance for distribution.

Twenty minutes before the screening, the member on duty should give a speech to instill civic knowledge and promote the New Life Movement.

If necessary during the screening, slides should be displayed, or the member on duty should explain.

The number of viewers should be limited to the number of seats in the cinema. Those who enter the venue in the middle of the screening should be refused.

Children who have not reached school age are not allowed to enter the venue. This should be clearly indicated in front of the door.

There should be a five-minute break for films that last more than forty minutes.

Reports on the results of each session should be prepared and sent to the Shanghai Children's Film Promotion Committee on a monthly basis for record-keeping.

The Chinese Fine Arts Association Will Hold Its Inaugural Meeting on Schedule This Sunday at the Chinese Arts and Crafts Society; Liu Haisu and Others Nominated as Presidium Members

The Chinese Fine Arts Association, initiated by more than 100 people in the art world, including Liu Haisu, Wang Jiyuan, and Xie Gongzhan, has been reported in various newspapers. The association has now been filed with the Party and government organs, and the preparatory work has been completed. It is scheduled to hold its inaugural meeting at 1:00 PM on the 15th of this month at the Chinese Arts and Crafts Society on Avenue Haig. Liu Haisu, Wang Jiyuan, and Jiang Jianbai have been nominated as members of the presidium for the meeting, and Cai Yuanpei, Sun Zhesheng, Wu Tiecheng, and Qin Liming have been invited to give speeches at the meeting. The details are as follows:

Purpose of the Initiative

Fine arts are the vitality of mankind, the repository of national spirit, and the object of national civilization. For thousands of years, our country's national culture has illuminated the world and continued to this day. Since the late modern era, under the impact of European capitalism, people only know how to compete for material possessions, enslaved by things and unable to break free. Trends are declining, and customs are becoming more vulgar. Our brilliant culture with thousands of years of history has been shaken and is in imminent danger. Recognizing that the revival of every nation must first go through a great ideological and artistic movement before it can succeed, as Italy, France, and Germany can attest to? Our country is in a precarious situation. Material civilization is very important, but spiritual civilization must not be ignored. There is also an urgent need for a great ideological movement to reverse the course of history. Therefore, this association is initiated to promote the glory of our country's inherent culture on the one hand and absorb the essence of European culture on the other hand, integrate them to create a new culture that is suitable for the world trend and our country's environment, to be the pioneer of human ideals and to lay the foundation for national civilization.

List of Initiators

Since the launch of the association, people from the art and education circles across the country have enthusiastically participated, including Liu Haisu, Wang Jiyuan, Ma Gongyu, Ni Yide, Xie Gongzhan, Lu Fengzi, Xie Haiyan, Liu Yazi, Jiang Jianbai, Chen Heqin, Gu Shusen, Wang Yuanbo, Yan Kechang, Gong Bizheng, Xu Xuangu, Bai Mingzhai, Liu Kang, Zhang Chengjiang, Pan Yuliang, Xiang Peiliang, Chen Renhao, Zheng Yuebo, Wang Yuejian, Zhou Duo, Ge Eryuan, Zheng Wuchang, Zhang Xian, Zhang Chongren, Liu Hairuo, Song Banggan, Wu Mengfei, and more than 100 others.

Scheduled Establishment

The association is scheduled to hold its opening ceremony at 1:00 PM on the afternoon of March 15th. After the ceremony, the meeting will continue to pass the constitution, elect officers, and discuss proposals. Liu Haisu, Wang Jiyuan, Jiang Jianbai, Ma Gongyu, Ni Yide, Xie Haiyan, Yan Kechang, Xie Gongzhan, Xiang Peiliang, Zhang Chengjiang, and Song Banggan have been nominated as officers of the meeting. Preparations are underway, and a grand occasion is expected at that time.

Children's Educational Novel

Little Men (Part 1) (9) (5)

— Original by Louisa M. Alcott, translated by Zheng Xiaocang

Dawn listened carefully to each question and answer. His heart leaped with joy at the thought of traveling to a new world with Mr. Hare. He also heard words of praise and recommendation, which made him feel that his recent efforts to live up to his friend's expectations had been rewarded. He was truly moved to tears.

After the gymnastics exercises, Xiaochiao and Tao Mo performed the famous comic play, "Money Makes the Devil Turn the Millstone." Xiaochiao did very well, and Tao Mo played the old farmer excellently, because his imitation of Director Lai made the audience laugh so hard they almost fell over. Even Director Lai himself couldn't stop laughing. Asia even patted him on the back a few times. They were standing in the hall, watching the hilarious play, and felt it was truly very interesting.

Amy waited until she had stopped laughing and could breathe, then went on stage, dressed as a sailor, and sang them a sea song, which included many things about "storms," "sheltered shores," and so on. Finally, everyone sang together, "Hoist the sails, friends, hoist the sails!" The sound shook the whole house. Afterwards, Nada put on a pagoda-pointed hat and performed a unique Chinese dance. Because there had never been any public exhibitions in Meizhuang, there were also some academic performances at this opportunity. The speed with which Xie Ke calculated on the blackboard was enough to astonish the audience. Tao Mo won first place in the spelling competition, and Xiaochiao read a French story so fluently and naturally that Uncle Tanti was very pleased in his heart.

When the curtain fell, everyone asked, "Where did the other little children go?"

At that time, Xiaochiao had already run to his mother's side, preparing to explain when the mystery gradually unfolded, but at this time he only said, "Ah, this is where the surprise comes in. It's really interesting, it's a pity you don't know."
