Shen Bao Medical and Pharmaceutical Special Issue

Overview of the Work of the Jiangsu Provincial Zhenjiang Rural Health Experiment Zone (3)

— Zhu Yun

After we arrived in Jianbi, we immediately contacted Liu Yuezhi, the director of the bureau, and all matters related to infant care and health management were handled by our office. Liu expressed great sympathy, and established an infant health experiment office in the bureau. We began to check the physical condition of wet nurses and the health of infants in the nursery. Infants fostered outside were scattered in 71 villages such as Caijia Village, Yinjia Village, and Liaoja Village. We conducted separate investigations, and sent nurses to visit and guide infant care and health knowledge. Those with diseases were treated. On the first, second, and third days of each month, a large number of foster mothers came to the infant receiving office to collect subsidies. We took advantage of the opportunity to give lectures on infant care and hygiene to the foster mothers. The listeners felt that it was relevant to their needs and closely related to themselves, so the effect was great. Physicians and nurses were sent to inspect the infants in the nursery in shifts every day, paying attention to the infants' daily life and the amount of milk fed by the wet nurses. The women who hired wet nurses and received infants had to undergo a physical examination by the physicians in our office. We also provided guidance on the matching and intake of daily nutrients for wet nurses.

B. Epidemic prevention work. 1. Children's vaccination: Vaccination can be carried out in all seasons of the year, but the general public is accustomed to waiting for the spring season to be vaccinated. Children in rural areas rarely have the opportunity to be vaccinated even in the spring season. At the beginning of our office's establishment, we purchased a large number of vaccine seedlings to vaccinate children in rural areas for free, and widely publicized the importance of autumn vaccination. In Jianbi Primary School, various private schools, and villages, a total of more than 500 children came to the clinic for vaccination. 2. Diphtheria prevention vaccination: In the transition between autumn and winter, the weather is dry and diphtheria is prone to spread. In order to prevent it in advance, we purchased a large number of diphtheria toxoids for free vaccination to the people in the township. We also printed a large number of publicity materials for extensive publicity. The Baojia chiefs notified the villagers in advance to receive injections at the office. At the same time, students in Jianbi Primary School were tested with the Schick test. Among the 96 students, 27 had a positive reaction and were given preventive vaccination.

C. Clinic work. In the Zhenjiang rural areas, which have suffered from years of famine and poor medical care, villagers suffer from two kinds of pain when they are sick: 1. They have no money to see a doctor and buy medicine; 2. They cannot find a skilled doctor. Therefore, our clinic work has won their great sympathy. It not only passively relieved many sick people who had no one to turn to, but also used this to connect the feelings of the villagers, making it much easier to promote health care, epidemic prevention, and other work. In four months, the clinic had a total of 3,223 outpatients, 1,173 initial visits, 2,050 return visits, 56 home visits, 25 emergency visits, 45 surgeries, and 295 injections. Among the various diseases, skin diseases were the most common, followed by digestive system diseases and respiratory system diseases.

D. Health education. 1. Mothers' Association. The Mothers' Association is the only group that promotes maternal and infant health and improves family hygiene, and we have received a lot of help. All women who have given birth to infants, regardless of age, are eligible to become members of the Mothers' Association. The association has three directors, who are elected by the members. The directors then elect one executive director to preside over the liaison between the members. Any group of ten members can form an association. Midwives and nurses from our office serve as instructors and hold discussion meetings once a month. 2. Farmer Caregiver Training Class. Take advantage of the farmers' leisure time to hold farmer caregiver training classes. The courses include: 1. Disease prevention methods; 2. Disease care methods; 3. Simple family treatment; 4. Infant care methods; 5. Vaccination methods; 6. Outline of bacteriology; 7. Principles of immunology; 8. Family hygiene; 9. Family entertainment; 10. First aid; 11. Practice. Classes are held for two hours each day and last for three weeks. It is held first in villages with more than 50 households. The first class was held in Xiaocun, and 46 women attended the class, with very few absences. After the completion of the training, a graduates' association was organized to facilitate the connection between the women in the whole village. 3. Family Hygiene Promotion Team. All staff members of our office formed a family hygiene promotion team and adopted a door-to-door promotion method. The promotion standards are divided into three categories: personal hygiene, family hygiene, and public hygiene. In terms of personal hygiene: 1. Do not drink raw water; 2. Do not put fingers into the ear canal or mouth, and do not rub the eyes; 3. Take a bath often; 4. Wash hands before meals and after going to the toilet; 5. Do not visit people with infectious diseases casually; 6. See a doctor for treatment when you are sick; 7. Do not sleep with your head covered; 8. Keep your nails trimmed; 9. Abstain from all bad habits; 10. Know how to get vaccinated. In terms of family hygiene: 1. The house should be ventilated; 2. The house should be cleaned every day; 3. The things in the house should be neat; 4. Clothes should be washed and changed often; 5. Face towels should be separated for each person; 6. Do everything possible to kill animals or insects with infectious diseases (flies, mosquitoes, rats, mad dogs); 7. Pay attention to the cleanliness of the source of drinking water; 8. Parents should supervise the family to get up early; 9. Do not engage in improper entertainment in the family; 10. Do not let children marry too early or too late; 11. Do not let children wear powder, pierce their ears, or bind their chests; 12. Do not keep coffins at home. In terms of public hygiene: 1. Do not wash toilets in the river; 2. Do not defecate or urinate anywhere; 3. Do not spit anywhere; 4. Do not throw away dead livestock anywhere; 5. Do not throw away garbage anywhere; 6. Do not bury coffins in the open air; 7. Notify neighbors if you have an infectious disease. This door-to-door promotion method brings hygiene knowledge to the door and is very effective. 3. Public speeches. The method of public speeches in rural areas is very simple, but the effect is great. We took a gong to a place, and when the gong rang, all the people in the village came. When speaking, the materials were simple and easy to understand, and mixed with various humorous and interesting anecdotes, so the listeners were very happy, and the speakers naturally felt very happy. 4. Masquerade performances. Using theatrical methods to promote hygiene has a deep impression and a great effect. A hygiene education troupe was specially organized. In addition to the staff of our office, students from Jianbi Qianwei Xiegou and other schools who are good at performing also participated. When performing in Qianwei Township, the audience reached 700 or 800 people, which was very popular for a while.

In just four months, we have only done a very small part of the entire plan. However, what we are proud of is that we did not ask the higher authorities for any operating expenses for the expenses incurred in health care, epidemic prevention, and treatment. At the same time, we did not collect donations from local people, but were completely helped and promoted by the people voluntarily. The people benefited from free childbirth and free medical care. The families with a little money all sent money (or things). We used it to buy cowpox vaccine, diphtheria toxoid, and other medicines. Recently, Liu Zhixian, a gentleman from Yuehu Township, donated ten acres and six and five-tenths of a cent of mountain land for our office to build a public platform. It has been reported to the Civil Affairs Department to order a commendation, and is cooperating with the county government to plan and establish a public cemetery. It can be seen that the people have automatically risen to assist in the promotion of health undertakings and are gradually moving towards the road of "health autonomy."

In terms of staff, Yuan Fanghai, Gao Yiliang, section chiefs, doctors, midwives, nurses, etc., are all very hardworking. Everyone wears cloth clothes, eats coarse food, and mingles with the people. I also stipulated that each person should have at least fifty friends who have received help in the countryside. I do the same myself. In the past few months, we have all achieved the ideal of making friends. Tangibly and intangibly, there are hundreds of people who are our helpers, which is of course beneficial to the advancement of the cause. January 1936, at the Zhenjiang Rural Health Experiment Zone Office

Resurrection from the Dead (Middle)

— Yue Qi

—Medical Story No. 18—

In addition, in the Connie area, there is a scientist named Professor Wider D. Bancroft, who is working hard to delay the arrival of death. According to him, a simple chemical called Sodium Rhodanate can increase a person's lifespan by at least two years. For people over the age of 45, this drug can prevent the hardening of their nerves and brain tissue, and can also increase their resistance to disease.

However, we have not heard of anything that has truly brought a dead person back to life. Dr. Connashi, encouraged by the success of the experiment on hounds, has gone one step further to attempt this. Currently, he is collecting the corpses of prisoners subjected to poisonous gas as experimental subjects. His plan is this. Move the corpse of the prisoner who has been declared dead by the doctor to the laboratory and tie it to the seesaw board. The second step is to inject a chemical called "methylene blue" into the venous tube to neutralize the poisonous gas. Pure oxygen is pumped into the lungs, and the seesaw board is slowly shaken to keep the blood circulating. The final step is to inject the life-giving liquid into the large vein. This liquid contains mostly fresh human blood and some adrenalin. This drug will cause the heart to contract violently, causing the still heart to beat again. Dr. Connashi is convinced that the dead will definitely come back to life after being injected with this liquid. He does not agree with the opinions of other scientists that the brain tissue of such resurrected people has suffered irreparable damage.

Brain and nerve tissue, unlike other special cells, are destroyed particularly quickly. An American scientist said that brain cells begin to decay immediately after the heart stops working. A French scientist set the time when brain cells begin to decay at 20 minutes after death. Many scientists therefore believe that even if the dead can be resurrected, he will definitely become disabled and useless. Dr. Connashi does not agree with this claim. The evidence he is based on is that the hound he experimented on remained as agile as before after being resurrected.

The method used by Dr. Connashi was unintentionally laid the foundation by a London doctor in 1855. This doctor's name is Dr. Thomas Addison, a doctor at the British Royal Hospital. He devoted himself to discovering a way to treat a strange disease. This strange disease—later called "Addison's disease"—affects the heart, causing the skin to turn copper-colored, and the pulse to be weak and irregular. Addison discovered that this disease was due to a lack of secretion from the adrenal glands. The adrenal glands are one of the human body's ductless glands, two inches long, located on the upper part of the kidneys. The secretory fluid of these adrenal glands, which was little known at the time, has a strange effect on the heart and blood vessels.

Since Addison announced this discovery, adrenal gland extracts have also been successfully manufactured by researchers. It was discovered that this extract also has a hemostatic function, so it is often used as an important drug in surgical medical rooms. However, this extract is difficult to last for a long time; it immediately loses its effectiveness when it comes into contact with air. Therefore, many scientists have devoted themselves to refining the elements of the adrenal glands, and the one who finally succeeded was the Japanese scientist Dr. Jokichi Takamine.

The element of the adrenal glands that has been successfully refined is a crystalline powder, white in color and bitter in taste. Its inventor named it adrenaline. This Japanese scientist passed away in 1922. At that time, he never dreamed that the adrenaline he had successfully manufactured would eventually accomplish an amazing miracle. It was not until 1923 that this miracle appeared in St. Louis Hospital in New York.

Common Sense Questions about Diseases

— Cheng Hanzhang

(79) Anemia (Continued)

Are there any abnormalities in the urine excreted by anemic patients?

The urine of anemic patients is large in quantity and transparent. The amount of urine excreted each day is 1.5 liters to 2 liters. The specific gravity is 1015-1021. Sometimes protein is found in the urine.

What changes will occur in the internal organs of people with severe anemia?

The heart, kidneys, blood vessels, etc. will all undergo fatty degeneration; especially the changes in blood vessels are more severe, and it is easy to bleed or moisture is easy to seep out, so edema or polyuria occurs.

Is the body temperature of anemic patients different from that of ordinary people?

In cases of severe anemia, fever occurs, with a temperature of 38.5 degrees Celsius to 39 degrees Celsius seen in the evening every day.

What is the reason for fever during anemia?

Because there are toxic protein bodies in the blood.

Is the number of red blood cells in the blood of anemic patients reduced?

Except for anemia caused by acute blood loss, the number of red blood cells in the blood is probably reduced by about 20%. That is, each cubic millimeter contains about 4 million.

Is the proportion of hemoglobin also reduced?

The amount of hemoglobin is also reduced by 40% to 50%.

Are there any changes in white blood cells in the blood of anemic patients?

There are generally no changes in white blood cells.

What is the prognosis of this disease, good or bad?

Generally good. As long as the cause is removed, it will gradually return to normal.

How to diagnose anemia?

First check the cause of the disease, then refer to what is seen in the blood; at the same time, check the stool for parasite eggs, and then the diagnosis can be confirmed.

What is the proper way to treat this secondary anemia?

The first is to treat the original disease. Use arsenic and iron preparations internally or by injection. Then use liver preparations internally or by injection. Eating liver (beef and pork liver) every day is also effective.

Children often suffer from anemia. What is the reason for this?

The causes of anemia in children are nothing more than prolonged breastfeeding, nutritional disorders, frequent consumption of milk substitutes, abnormal physique, lack of vitamin foods, or congenital syphilis or tuberculosis, or parasites in the intestines.

What are the symptoms of anemia in children?

Children with anemia have yellowish skin, no blood color in their cheeks, enlarged spleen, and the blood findings are similar to those of secondary anemia in adults; however, white blood cells are increased.

What is the treatment for anemia in children?

The treatment of anemia in children should focus on diet therapy, eating more vegetables and fruits containing vitamins, and liver. In addition, they should often be in places with plenty of sunlight and fresh air, or irradiated with artificial sun lamps. Sometimes blood transfusion therapy is performed. Arsenic and iron preparations can also be used, but caution should be taken.

Domestic Medicinal Plants (Continued)

— Zhou Mengbai

(19) Sunflower Heliauthus Aununs, L.

Sounenblume (German) Sunflower (English)

(Plant) Originally produced in North America, it can be cultivated everywhere. It is an annual grass. The stem is 1-3 meters high, and the whole plant is densely covered with bristles. The leaves are alternate, petiolate, broad and large, broadly ovate, with coarsely serrated edges and acute tips. In summer and autumn, terminal capitate flowers are produced, and the ligulate flowers are yellow. The achene is obovate.

(Composition) The composition of achenes (seeds) is as follows. Moisture 3.3.12.8%, nitrogenous substances 12.51.19.1%, fatty oil 22.2.36.5%, nitrogen-free organic matter 13.3.21.3%, crude fiber 23.5.32.3%, ash 2.6.4.1%. The fatty oil is mainly composed of glycerol trioleate (Olein).

(Uses) Sunflower fatty oil can be used as edible oil. It can also be used as a raw material for stone, paint, etc.

(20) Tussilaginea Ligularia, Makino.

(Plant) It grows naturally by the sea in warm areas, or is planted in gardens. It is a perennial grass with greenery. The leaves are radical, with long petioles, leathery, kidney-shaped, with wavy edges. The petioles and the back of the leaves are densely covered with brown wool. In autumn, the flower stalks are drawn out, and the terminal capitate flowers are yellow.

(Composition) The roots contain Senecioaure.

(Medicinal) Folk: It is said that the stems and leaves have the effect of detoxifying fish, that is, if puffer fish or carp is poisoned, the leaves can be decocted or the juice of the raw leaves can be squeezed and taken internally. For suppuration, eczema, etc., rub the leaves to soften them, lightly bake them with fire, and apply them to the affected area.

(21) Siegesbeckia Pubescens. Makino

(Plant) It grows naturally in the wilderness and is an annual grass. The stem is 1--1.5 meters high, and the whole plant is densely covered with short hair. The leaves have thorns, are ovate-circular, with irregular jagged edges and sharp tips. Terminal conical inflorescences produce capitate flowers in autumn.

(Composition) According to the composition of this plant, there is still no research, but the near species S. Orientalis, L. contains the bitter substance Darutin.

(Medicinal) It is said that the leaves can relieve malignant sores, swelling poison, rheumatism, and stroke are also effective.

Tooth Knowledge Q&A (23)

— Lin Jianxian

(Question 112) How should children who like to eat sweets protect their teeth?

Answer: Teach him to brush his teeth every time after eating to wash away the remaining food debris. At least, he must rinse his mouth a lot to rinse away the residue.

(Question 113) What should children pay attention to during the period of changing teeth?

Answer: Milk teeth should not be extracted early before the time of changing teeth to avoid uneven growth of adult teeth, which are prone to decay. However, when it is time to change, and they feel very wobbly, they should be extracted immediately, and they must not be left in place to hinder the growth of adult teeth; otherwise, the adult teeth will inevitably be uneven and prone to decay.

(Question 114) Should the upper and lower alveolar ridges of children be straightened when they are uneven?

Answer: If there are irregularities in the upper and lower alveolar ridges, it is not only unsightly, but also occludes unevenly, and it is easy to cause cavities, so you should ask a dentist to correct them as soon as possible.

(Question 115) Does the protection of milk teeth require the help of a dentist?

Answer: Even if children pay attention to oral hygiene and protect their teeth at all times, they may still develop cavities. These cavities are usually very small, painless, and cannot be found by themselves. It is best to ask a dentist to check them once every six months, and if there are any cavities, they can be repaired immediately to avoid them getting bigger and bigger. Nowadays, in many foreign schools, children are under the strict supervision and guidance of dentists, who pay considerable attention to their oral hygiene methods and diet, and regularly check their teeth and record them in forms, which can be consulted at any time. It is said that people who are under such supervision have better teeth and are rarely incomplete in adulthood.

(Question 116) Are there any simple methods that can be used to prevent the erosion of milk teeth?

Answer: Silver nitrate can be used to apply to the occlusal surface of the milk teeth every six months. That is, after the first and second permanent molars have grown, they can also be applied together. Even if children are around ten years old, if they feel that there is a tendency for cavities, it is also appropriate to use this medicine to apply to the surface of all teeth once a year or every six months. After the application, try to make the silver precipitate. If there is a place where cavities are starting, it will be dyed black. The larger the cavities, the deeper the coloring. Therefore, this method can not only curb the progress of cavities, but also discover small cavities that are not easily detected by ordinary means.

Ear, Nose, Throat, and Eye Disease Hygiene Knowledge

— Tang Renjin

(80) Eczema and Frostbite of the Auricle

Auricular Eczema: Auricular eczema mostly occurs in children. Its causes can be divided into three categories: When suffering from chronic otorrhea, the flowing pus can often irritate the auricle, causing eczema. It can also be secondary to eczema of the head. Drug irritation from substances such as iodoform, mercuric chloride, aluminum acetate, lead sugar, and boric acid can also cause eczema. This disease has a tendency to repeatedly recur in patients with glandular diathesis. Its common sites are generally the opening of the external auditory canal and its vicinity, the hollows between the auricle's convolutions, and the folds between the auricle and the mastoid process.

The symptoms of auricular eczema are generally the same as those of common skin eczema. Patients feel itchy. The skin of the auricle becomes red and moist. Crusts or pustules may also form, or the epidermis may peel off. Painful swelling or suppuration often occurs in the lymph nodes behind the ear or in the superficial cervical lymph nodes. The treatment for auricular eczema requires, first and foremost, addressing the underlying cause. Chronic otorrhea or eczema of the head should be treated first, and drug irritation should be avoided. The rest of the treatment is the same as for common skin eczema.

Auricular Frostbite: In the severe winter and early spring, we often inevitably suffer from frostbite. The most easily affected parts are the hands, feet, and auricles. Its pain is unbearable. The most easily frostbitten part of the auricle is the upper posterior margin of the helix. Mild frostbite only causes loss of sensation in the helix due to vasoconstriction. Moderate frostbite causes itching or pain due to vasoparalysis. Severe frostbite can cause blisters or ulcers, and even lead to gangrene.

Prevention of auricular frostbite involves protecting the auricle and avoiding cold air exposure. As for its treatment, it is generally the same as for frostbite of the hands and feet.

A Brief Discussion of Pulmonary Tuberculosis (84)

— Hu Jiayan

Section 8 Surgical Treatment

The adoption of surgical treatment for pulmonary tuberculosis is undoubtedly a major advancement in modern treatment! In the initial stages, the indications were not fully understood, and the surgical methods were not entirely appropriate. Therefore, according to recent clinical reports, on average, at least fifteen out of one hundred patients undergo surgical treatment. Among these patients who have undergone surgery, roughly two-thirds can achieve considerable results. This figure is, of course, relative and limited, far from being as effective as diphtheria antitoxin in treatment. However, even considering this partial success, its greatness in benefiting humanity is worthy of praise!

What is surgical treatment? What principle is it based on? We know that if people's lungs are compressed by external pressure, their tissues can become atrophic. Based on clinical observations, patients with this disease often have natural pneumothorax or exudative pleurisy, and their lung tissue is often in a compressed state. The prognosis of these cases is mostly better than others. Based on this principle, in modern treatment of pulmonary tuberculosis, "artificial pneumothorax" surgery has been adopted! It involves injecting an appropriate amount of air into the patient's chest cavity. At this time, the alveoli are compressed, blood flow stagnates, and the lungs cannot easily expand during breathing. Indirectly, it makes it difficult for lesions within the lung tissue to spread, and the healthy tissues are also compressed by the air, and the stagnation of blood flow can promote the proliferation of new connective tissue. The lesion can also be healed by scarring. Even cavities in the lungs can be healed by scarring. Therefore, although this surgical treatment is clearly not the bactericidal specific therapy we dream of, it promotes scarring of the lesion and the proliferation of connective tissue around the lesion, ultimately leading the patient towards recovery. We can boldly say that this clinical result achieves the same effect as an ideal bactericidal specific therapy.

What types of cases are suitable for artificial pneumothorax surgery? First, we must understand that most patients who need artificial pneumothorax surgery are severely ill. For mild cases of this disease, it is not necessary, with the exception of early cavities. In terms of the nature of the disease, the proliferative type is most suitable, followed by the proliferative-exudative type. The purely exudative type mostly yields poor results. In summary, its most suitable type is severe, progressive, proliferative, and unilateral disease. It is also deemed necessary for patients with cavities! In addition, for patients with recurrent hemoptysis, if the lesion is unilateral, it is also one of the most suitable indications. Patients can generally be saved from danger. Regarding lesions limited to one side or spread to both sides, doctors previously believed that artificial pneumothorax surgery was completely impossible for bilateral disease. Doctors must be completely clear about a unilateral case before proceeding. Now, the scope of indications has gradually expanded. Even for tuberculosis in both lungs, surgery can sometimes be performed! This is worth reporting! As for complications such as intestinal tuberculosis, spondylitis, bilateral kidney tuberculosis, emphysema, asthma, severe diabetes, severe nephritis, and valvular heart disease, as well as patients who are excessively weak, artificial pneumothorax surgery is very unsuitable and falls into the category of contraindications. In addition, conditions like laryngeal tuberculosis and unilateral kidney tuberculosis are not absolute contraindications. If the ulceration in the larynx is not severe, and the general condition of patients with kidney tuberculosis is still good, surgery can still be performed.

Guangdong Mill Continues to Decline by 0.3 Cents in the Black Market

Call Loan Rate Remains Fixed at 8%

Foodstuffs: Germany's Abrogation of Treaty Actually Causes Large-Scale Speculation in Coarse Grains

If war breaks out in Europe, the export of oil beans and sesame seeds will certainly be impacted, while the import of foreign wheat into China will be hindered. Wheat flour, oil beans, bean cakes, and sesame seeds will all rise in price.

Prices of standard oil beans, bean cakes, and sesame seeds in various cities all soared yesterday. Although there was no large-scale purchasing by customers or foreign firms, the market sentiment was universally optimistic. This was because Dalian telegrams had repeatedly indicated good prices. Given reports that German troops were on the move, the possibility of war breaking out in Europe seemed imminent. Speculative buying suddenly surged in the market. According to Dalian telegrams, there was also speculative buying by certain parties in that region. In Shanghai, in addition to the rush to buy at floating profits, there was also speculation from outside the industry. The general consensus was that if war broke out in Europe, there would definitely be a large outflow of oil beans and sesame seeds to foreign firms. Moreover, current arrivals were not plentiful, and local sales were still active, with a solid foundation. Therefore, prices rose for all near and distant months. Foreign sesame seeds rose sharply by 1.80 yuan per dan (unit of volume), standard beans rose sharply by 1.10 yuan per dan, near-term oil rose by nearly 4 yuan, and long-term oil rose by 6-7 yuan.

The yellow bean market situation was such that spot soybean oil was extremely scarce, and the market was tense. Moreover, bean cake sales were brisk and active, with all factories producing over 40,000 pieces of various brands of cake, and the market price suddenly looked promising. Therefore, the raw materials for oil cake were able to continue to thrive. Yesterday, the market saw the Luohe Bean Factory dispatch 2,000 bags at a price of 5.10 yuan. The Quanzhou merchants transacted 100 bags at a price of 5.03 yuan. Furthermore, the Bengbu Bean Factory acquired 400 bags, and the Zhumadian Bean Factory acquired 300 bags. In addition, they ordered seven cartloads of Tongliao beans from the inland route at a price of 5 yuan. The Shantou and Xiamen merchants were actively purchasing sand yellow and Du beans from this street, with a total of 2,600 bags transacted. The price of high-grade sand yellow had reached 5 yuan, and the price of high-quality Du beans had also increased by 3-4 fen.

After the opening of the flour market in the morning, there was a consistent positive trend. Foreign wheat quotations showed gains of 3-5 jiao in Chicago and around 4 jiao in Canada. Market sentiment was nervous due to the changing situation in Europe, and there was a belief that war might break out. Therefore, near-term customers were pulling in stock, and long-term speculative buyers from outside the industry were aggressively buying in, resulting in a greater increase. By the afternoon opening, the market sentiment for the current month turned stable due to factories selling off their holdings. However, due to concerns about the uncertainty of future foreign wheat prices, the buying interest in new flour starting from June remained strong, and market prices continued to increase by 2 fen. As a result, near-term prices rose by 1-2 fen, and long-term prices rose significantly by 4-5 fen.

After the opening of the wheat market in the morning, prices for all months rose sharply. Foreign wheat quotations rebounded by around 3-5 jiao. Furthermore, due to the European crisis and fears of future expansion, the general sentiment was that foreign wheat might not be available for purchase. Therefore, the opening price for the current month remained relatively stable, while trading in the long-term was very active, and prices also rose sharply by as much as 7-8 fen. The majority of buyers consisted of outside-industry speculators, while those in the industry mostly sold out. By the afternoon opening, arrivals for the current month were very few, while trading in the long-term remained brisk, with large fluctuations. Observing future trends will depend on international developments. Trading in the current wheat market was not active, with only 900 bags transacted. Shandong wheat was priced at 5.23 yuan, and Tiantai wheat was priced at 5.20 yuan, acquired by the Fu, Fu, and Shen companies.

The Jiangxi early and late indica rice, which various merchants had been vying for in recent days, only saw some response from merchants on this street and from Nanjing and Quanzhou. Finance in the Past Year (Continued 3)

— He Boxiong

4. Foreign Exchange

China's exchange market is centered in Shanghai, so fluctuations in silver prices are reflected in Shanghai first. The following table summarizes the relationship between overseas silver prices and Shanghai exchange rates in recent years to provide a glimpse. (Note 4)

Attached: Table of Silver Price and Exchange Rate Fluctuations in Recent Years

Notes: New York silver prices are in US cents per ounce, London silver prices are in pence per ounce, New York exchange rates are in US dollars per 100 silver yuan, London exchange rates are in pence per silver yuan, and silver surplus and deficit are in yuan.

Since the 21st year, exchange rates for British and American currencies have gradually risen along with the increase in overseas silver prices. By May of the 24th year, the British exchange rate had risen to 20.125 pence, and the American exchange rate had risen to 40.971 US dollars. If the American exchange rate in the 21st year is taken as 100, then the exchange rate in the 22nd year actually increased by 21.51%, the exchange rate in the 23rd year actually increased by 57.22%, and the exchange rate in May of last year actually increased by 90.22%. Although the exchange rate increased so much, it still lagged behind the increase in silver prices. The silver price in New York in the 22nd year was 22.28% higher than in the 21st year, the silver price in the 23rd year was 69.12% higher than in the 21st year, and the silver price in May of the 24th year was 162.74% higher than in the 21st year. The exchange rates for British and Japanese currencies were generally the same as for American currency. The rise in silver prices was so rapid, and China's international balance of payments was in a negative situation, so silver flowed out in large quantities. The surplus in the 21st year was over 10 million yuan, which increased to over 14 million yuan in the 22nd year. By the end of the 23rd year, the silver surplus had reached over 254 million yuan. This was all because overseas silver prices were far higher than the increase in China's foreign exchange, creating a difference, and thus creating opportunities for profit. Actual silver was then continuously transported to Britain and the United States. Since January of last year, silver has had a surplus of 1-2 million yuan each month. This is because a large amount of silver had already flowed out domestically, leading to a depleted reserve. The Price Stabilization Committee then sold cash and purchased silver to adjust the market. Looking at the cash import and export statistics table from January to June of last year (there were no imports or exports from July to October), the large surplus of gold can be seen.

Chronicles

Tidbits

— (Yi Zhi)

The knowledge that young people need now must be able to critically assess "whether," otherwise, it will be as useless as being blind. It is also impossible to be a warrior in a dark society.

Some people say: A person's self-confidence should not be too strong. Yes, a person's wisdom is limited. Although a person is usually very smart, there are many times when they will become a first-rate fool and do things that are more foolish than anyone else.

"Smart for a lifetime, foolish for a moment." The great Newton also made many mistakes, and his friends and servants pointed them out to him! So, is the intelligent Newton not as good as his servant?

From this point of view, a person's self-confidence should indeed not be too strong, because sometimes your thoughts will also be wrong, and things will also be done wrong. If you only deeply believe in yourself, it is also unreliable.

In short, self-confidence should not be too strong, nor can it be absent. It is best to think three times before acting.

Talking about Leap Months

— Aimei

February of this year in the Western calendar has 29 days, which is a leap year. I suppose that at the beginning of setting the calendar, there may not have been a scientific basis, so the construction of the months, the remainder of the year, and the intercalary days were all based on rigid formulas. However, the ancient calendar of our country is not like that. In its method of calculation, it studies the heavens above and infers the earth's atmosphere below. Ordinary people only say that it is calculated according to the movements of the sun and moon, but that does not fully explain its principles.

Taking just the leap month system as an example, according to the Zuo Zhuan Commentary: "The month combines with the monthly node. Each month combines with one day. All remaining days are returned to the end, forming a month, which is then placed as a leap month." Also, Ban Gu's Bai Hu Tong says: "The Zhou sky has 365 and a quarter degrees. The year has twelve months. The sun passes twelve degrees per month, so there is one leap month every three years and another addition every five years, clarifying that yin is insufficient and yang is surplus." This is indeed an explanation of why leap months are set, and everyone knows it. However, Lu Ji's Theory of the Celestial Sphere says: "The leap month has no middle energy, and the Big Dipper points obliquely between two zodiacal signs, so it is different from other months." This means that the calendar is related to the stars in addition to the sun and moon, so there is such a response in the year of the leap month!

As for the signs corresponding to the Earth's atmosphere, flowers and trees can all be used for verification. The "Miscellaneous Records" says: "Boxwood is firm and grows slowly, growing one inch per year, and reversing one inch in the leap year." It also says: "The Chinese parasol tree can know the correct positions of the sun and moon, growing twelve leaves. One side has six leaves, counted from the bottom. One leaf represents one month, and if there is a leap month, it will grow thirteen leaves. By looking at the smallest leaf, one can know which month is the leap month." It also says: "Lotus roots grow according to the months, with one node growing per month. In the leap month, one more node is added." Furthermore, the Yunnan Zhi says: "The He Mountain flower is similar to cassia, with twelve petals per flower, corresponding to the twelve months. When there is a leap month, it has one more petal." It also says: "The udumbara flower is shaped like a lotus, with twelve petals. When there is a leap month, it has one more petal. This flower is white and fragrant, and comes from the Western Regions (probably referring to Buddhist India). It is also a type of sal flower." These are all evidences.

I have also heard that the tail feathers of the rainbow phoenix are also related to the calendar. The Yu Mao Kao Yi says: "The phoenix has twelve tail feathers, and when there is a leap month, it grows thirteen tail feathers." Below it also discusses music, saying: "The coda of today's small tunes in the Music Bureau has twelve beats, symbolizing the phoenix's tail, so it is called the coda. Or four words are added, also adding one beat, symbolizing the leap month." Writing this, I recall that there were many ancient musical systems that symbolized time, not just this, such as the zither. The Wen Xian Tong Kao says: "The zither has five strings, corresponding to the five tones; twelve strings, corresponding to the twelve musical laws; and a thirteen-stringed one, of which one string symbolizes the leap month."

Our country's agricultural affairs often follow the calendar, and in leap years, the timing must be late. The Qi Min Yao Shu says: "In general, fields should be mixed with early and late planting. In a leap year, the solar terms are later, so it is appropriate to plant late fields." This is why Dai Shulun's poem has the line "In the leap year, the crops are late." If we follow the Western system, we will lose our basis. Therefore, although the government has abolished the ancient calendar, it still shows people the new moons, full moons, and solar terms in order to benefit agriculture.

Other things that can be discussed are: the meaning of the character "潤" (run, leap), which is a unique structure. According to the Three Dynasties: "The Son of Heaven lived in the main hall of the Zongzhang, with his own room each month, but in the leap month, he ordered the king to live at the door, so the character "潤" (run) is composed of "王" (wang, king) and "門" (men, door)." The commentary on the Zhou Li explains it this way.

The Servant of a Broad and Generous Heart

—

Kiln Workers

— Danxia

Kilns are distinguished as porcelain kilns, lime kilns, brick and tile kilns, etc. What is described below is limited to brick and tile kilns.

Where there are kilns, there is often a saying: "Big saws in the city, big buns (i.e., big steamed buns) in the countryside." They liken the city walls to saws and the kiln mounds to buns, which is quite accurate. Therefore, the most difficult part of building a kiln mound is the top surface that forms a dome. This is definitely not something ordinary plasterers can do; one must hire the so-called "kiln building supervisor." There are usually about four people, and their wages are particularly generous, and they are also treated to a full-course meal, which ordinary kiln workers envy.

In peacetime, there are tasks such as "loading the kiln," "firing the kiln," "fetching water," and "unloading the goods." Among them, the "kiln loading supervisor" has a relatively important responsibility. It is their job to economically arrange the clay blanks into the kiln. This also requires skilled operations, of course; and if the loading is uneconomical or the distribution is inappropriate, the fired bricks and tiles will be fewer in number and of much lower quality. This is very different from the interests of the kiln owners.

In addition, there are general female workers who are hired temporarily. -- Although they are said to be hired temporarily, they actually have a very strict organization, and others are not easily allowed to join the work. -- They are only used for "carrying blanks" and "unloading goods." They are collectively called "blank-carrying goddesses." The wages are only about 200 wen each time, and they are mostly young women. When a boatload of blanks arrives at the kiln yard, as soon as someone shouts loudly, they gather from all directions. They shuttle back and forth on the kiln yard like shuttles, their voices are clear and lively. When it comes to "unloading the goods," they put on their old work clothes, which are patched up with thousands of stitches, in advance, preparing to wrestle with the black kiln ash. When the work is over, they are all black all over, and they can't find any clean skin on their faces, leaving only a pair of dark, shining eyes and half-points of blood-red lips. Fortunately, people are used to it, and even if they walk among people, they are not surprised at all. This is also a type of occupation for ordinary women.

Little Western Paradise

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 24: Lured by Profit, the Base Man Breaks Love; With High Aspirations and Healthy Feet, the Strong Man Flees to the Wilderness

Old Man Zhang laughed and said: Teacher Cheng, why would a smart person like you ask us such a question? May I ask, if they aren't officials, who can live in Little Western Paradise? We built the houses in Little Western Paradise with our own hands. After the houses were built, we people in tattered clothes were not allowed to enter. Isn't it right that people should be officials? Zhiqian looked at him and nodded twice, saying: You are right. If this Mr. Wang becomes an official, he will definitely repay you for helping him. What do you hope he will repay you with? Old Man Zhang raised his hand, scratched his scalp, and shook his head with a smile, saying: What should I have him repay me with? I'm so old, what comfort do I want to seek? I think, if Mr. Wang becomes an official in the future, he can set a regulation for our mud and wood workers, giving an extra one or two mao of wages to people over fifty years old. That would be a great merit. Teacher Cheng, you don't know, the effort of an old man is different from that of a young man. When they are working, they are already gritting their teeth. After the work is done, when they return home, they really don't want to say a word. Lying on the kang at night, they have a big illness, constantly shivering. Zhiqian nodded, saying: You are a benevolent person. People in this world always help each other. As long as you handle Mr. Wang's affairs well, I don't think Mr. Wang will let you down. Even if I act as a go-between, seeing your strength, I can't help but thank you. Old man, just go and do what you have prepared. Saying that, he walked closer to him, lightly patting Old Man Zhang's shoulder with his hand, expressing that close and classless meaning between the two of them. This time, it directly encouraged Old Man Zhang to become exuberant, and he puffed out his chest and said: Teacher Cheng, don't look at me being so old, I have a cavity full of hot blood, as long as I sell it to someone who knows the goods. Saying that, he stretched out his palm and clapped his chest several times in a row. Cheng Zhiqian said: Your sense of righteousness has raised my spirits quite a bit. Old Man Zhang said: Teacher Cheng, just tell me, what else do you want me to do? If I am even a little ambiguous, you Teacher Cheng can consider that you have wrongly recognized me. Zhiqian looked at his face, smiled, and then nodded, saying: I don't have anything else, it's still for other people. Didn't you hear that Sister-in-Law Hu is still there whimpering, wanting to sell someone else's flesh and blood? This can only be said with justice by a local old man like you, to suppress him. (413)

Stones from Other Hills

Military Training of Japanese Students

— Ji Yun

In Japan, from middle school to vocational school, there is a subject called physical education, which is military training, about two hours a week. In addition to military training, middle schools also have gymnastics. However, schools above vocational schools only have military training and no gymnastics. The student army in our country's universities is famously composed of young masters. Taking off their smart suits and having to wear cloth military uniforms makes many people unhappy. What's more, having to practice with iron guns is even more exhausting. On weekdays, they shout loudly to save the country, but as soon as they have an iron gun in their hands, they feel the hardship, and it is definitely not as easy as saving the country with empty words.

Japanese students sometimes get lazy and absent from academic subjects. However, attendance at military training is compulsory. If there are too many absences, the score will fail, and there is even a risk of repeating the grade. In other subjects, they can whisper to each other in the classroom, or be more casual. However, as soon as the instructor arrives, everyone's face becomes serious, and their bodies straighten up. They have to endure for an hour without freedom. The instructors are all from the military, mostly school officers, and many have participated in wars. They are so familiar with the Chinese map drawn on the blackboard that even our country's geography teachers would be ashamed of themselves. They are even more familiar with the geography of the three northeastern provinces. They know what fortresses are there, what rivers there are, and roughly how many miles there are. They know how the Russo-Japanese War was fought. They know where the Manchurian Incident killed how many people. They know every winding village like the back of their hands. When they are in the lecture hall, in addition to teaching the infantry manual, they mostly lecture on the actual situation of previous wars.

The uniform for Japanese military training is different from the student uniform. It is made of yellowish-green cloth, and each set costs only a little more than three yuan. When practicing, they also have to add bayonets, ammunition boxes, and leggings. Except for rainy days when teaching in the lecture hall, there has been no interruption regardless of the cold or warmth. Recently, Japan has been unusually cold, with mornings as cold as six degrees below zero, but military training is still held. The instructors wear wool military uniforms, long military boots, and white gloves. The students' uniforms are thin, so they can't wear gloves. Standing in the wind, both legs are shivering.

There is at least one field exercise every year, usually in the suburbs of Tokyo. It lasts about three or four days, and each person has to pay a fee of four or five yuan. They often see students carrying guns on the road, which means that they are going to the gathering place. Last year, the Tokyo official middle school practiced with tanks, field guns, airplanes, etc., which is obviously much more advanced than our country. They have a conscription system, and everyone has an obligation to serve in the army, so military training for students is even more common. Several students were suddenly notified to join the army while they were studying, so they had to stop studying at any time and go to the army. The tuition fees for those few months can be waived.

The military training instructor also serves as a student supervisor, which is of course stricter than our country's dean of students. He manages all the students' actions and handles absences and requests for leave. Japanese students are respectful to him, and stricter instructors even force students to shave their heads like monks. The preparatory students of Keio University once caused a disturbance because of this. The reason why Japanese students all have shaved heads is because of military training. Our country's students only shave their heads for a few months during joint training, and they are already very lucky.

Miscellaneous Words

Idle Chat on Storytelling with Drums

— Huang Baihong

Storytelling with drums was originally called "drum lyrics," referring to the general term for singing stories accompanied by a flat drum. The flat drum isn't very large, hence the reason for calling it "big drum" stems from the fact that drum lyrics used to specialize in performing lengthy stories, such as Romance of the Three Kingdoms and Water Margin. Nowadays, the performances have all become shorter segments, no longer using large sets, and should be properly called "drum storytelling."

Drum storytelling is a product of the Yellow River basin, having been introduced by farmers and spreading from villages and towns into cities. In the past, during times of peace and prosperity, people would gather in open spaces to listen to storytelling during their leisure time after farming. The drum (therefore the drum was short-legged) even used discarded farm tool iron pieces as accompanying instruments. To this day, the "plow blade pieces" mentioned in Shandong, Henan, and other places still have traces that can be found. However, once it entered the cities, it had to follow the refined taste. Thus, "plow blade pieces," due to similar pronunciation, became "pear blossom drums." Nevertheless, the flat drum was still short-legged, only the iron pieces were changed to copper pieces; the original appearance can only be imagined. Therefore, many people believe that drum storytelling originated in Shandong, and the current so-called pear blossom drum is the ancestor of drum storytelling.

The old capital, Beijing, used to be the model area of the country. Once drum storytelling entered the capital, the short-legged drum transformed into a high-stand drum, and the copper pieces became small sandalwood clappers; and the tone also changed from crude to refined. Therefore, a separate school was formed, which is the "even tone big drum."

Currently, the types of drum storytelling, in terms of region, can be divided into even tone (also written as even rhyme tune) big drum, Shandong big drum, and Fengtian big drum. Generally speaking, there are only two categories: even tone big drum and pear blossom drum. (Note that Shandong, Fengtian, etc., all belong to the pear blossom drum.) In terms of tone and lyrics, the even tone big drum has reached perfection, clear and pleasing to the ear; the pear blossom iron pieces inevitably have too much rustic air, so the orthodox of drum storytelling is now considered to be the even tone big drum.

Performers of the pear blossom drum variety are mostly female, while the even tone big drum has both male and female performers, but most of the masters are male. This is probably because drum storytelling requires physical performance, and women's spirit is ultimately not as strong as men's. As for the tone of pear blossom drum, it is fundamentally upright, and when sung by women, it can be neutralized, but when performed by men, it is rather rough.

In addition, there is the octagonal drum, which is said to have been the exclusive entertainment of the Eight Banner people, originating from the victory songs of the banner soldiers. Strictly speaking, it should not belong to the category of big drum. The plum blossom tune (now commonly known as plum blossom big drum) is said to belong to the octagonal drum category, but all the instruments used are the same as the big drum, and there is usually a single-stringed instrument in the middle. The Taiping ballad is sung a cappella without stringed instruments. (Note that the above mostly belong to Beijing tones.)

Speaking of the material of drum storytelling, much of it is taken from opera: such as Nanyang Pass, Changban Slope, Huarong Road, Farewell Mother with a Barrage of Arrows, etc. In modern times, Peking opera became popular, so some drum lyrics inserted Peking opera tunes: Ma'anshan, Ziqi Listening to the Qin, adding Erhuang; Empty City Stratagem, Nanyang Pass, adding Xipi, etc. (Thus, there is even a clever establishment of names, called Peking Opera Drum.) Even the physical performances during singing are inseparable from the flavor of opera. Furthermore, in general lyrics, some words and tunes can be found at any time. Therefore, some people believe that some of the lyrics in drum storytelling are very similar to Yuan Dynasty songs. It is likely that some of the drum lyrics were written by scholars, but most of the authors did not reveal their names, so few people know about it. Among them, only Han Xiaochuang and Jia Weishan are relatively famous. Jia was from Jining, Shandong, and his drum lyrics were compiled and printed into a book called "Wooden Skin Lyrics."

I am completely ignorant of lyrics and music and dare not act as an interpreter. However, I certainly love to listen to drum storytelling. I think drum lyrics have literary characteristics: first, the interest is moderate; second, the style is strict; third, it is close to spoken language. Therefore, I believe that drum storytelling has a great future. I hope that seniors with literary cultivation and those who are good at lyrics and music will participate in researching and improving it.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talk

Don't Hope in Others

— Tan

After the major explosion in Japan, their outcome is still difficult to predict at this point. However, the occurrence of an incident is bound to be due to a dispute between two factions, resulting in the defeat of the moderate faction and the victory of the radical faction, the defeat of the literary faction and the victory of the military faction. This statement can be said to be the rule for any incident.

The average newspaper reader and those who care about national affairs are frightened upon hearing of the Japanese incident, as if a major disaster is about to arrive. Hearing that Hirota received the imperial order to form a cabinet, they are delighted, thinking that they can rest easy from now on, because Hirota is a key figure who advocates a policy of peace and does not advocate a scorched-earth policy. Their delight is understandable. However, Hirota's cabinet formation was met with disapproval from the military, causing setbacks. Thus, a newspaper stated, "Since the occurrence of the incident, the political situation surrounded by an atmosphere of unease was about to release a glimmer of dawn, but unexpectedly, the evil currents rising from the military suddenly expanded, and the smooth and easy birth of the new cabinet is about to sail onto a reef." People cannot help but feel fear again.

Naturally, the origin of this sudden change in Japan, triggered by the suggestion of what kind of people, is undoubtedly clear. Now that Hirota has formed a cabinet, Hayashi Senjuro, Shinzaki, Abe, and Araki have been ordered to resign. Even if this situation temporarily appeases the situation, there may still be unfortunate consequences in the future. Therefore, a newspaper stated that Hirota's resignation from the imperial order to form a cabinet is only a matter of time (reported on the 6th). According to a report from the 7th Allied Press, Hirota's meeting with Terauchi resulted in the new cabinet being formed today. All in all, even if Hirota's cabinet formation succeeds, it will definitely not be Hirota's cabinet.

Therefore, I dare to conclude that the radical faction will not fail and the moderate faction will not prevail in this Japanese incident. Furthermore, I will say that no matter which faction fails and which faction prevails, it will absolutely not benefit our country. In short, this internal dispute of opinions in Japan has nothing to do with our country. The difference between so-called moderation and radicalism is only the difference in methods and means, while their fundamental propositions are consistent.

The same criminal, the scorched-earth policy uses the method of shooting or beheading to resolve the matter, while the peace policy uses the method of slow slicing or standing cage. The means of execution may vary in urgency, but the declaration of the death penalty for the criminal is the same. Therefore, we should stand firm, make up our minds, and set our steps. Whether they use a scorched-earth policy or a peace policy, we should deal with the scorched-earth policy with scorched-earth means, and deal with the peace policy with peaceful means. Otherwise, the scorched-earth policy is frightening, but isn't the peace policy also frightening? The scorched-earth policy is dangerous, but isn't the peace policy also dangerous? Therefore, I fundamentally do not hope in others.

Field Frog

— Hua Mu

——One of the Spring Delicacies of the Hometown——

It is not easy to eat field frogs in Shanghai. They are rarely seen in fresh food stalls and are only available in Guangdong seafood stores around North Sichuan Road and Wuchang Road. People in Shanghai do not like the field frog dishes sold in restaurants because the meat does not taste good. People with delicate stomachs may not even be able to swallow it. We, who have tasted the delicious flavor of field frogs in our hometown, can easily tell the difference between good and bad and cannot be fooled.

Field frogs in our hometown are one of the precious foods, selling for a high price. One yuan can only buy four or five fat ones. There are many ways to cook them. Stir-frying, braising, stewing, boiling, and red-braising all have their own unique flavors. The skin and meat are tender and fresh, and the bones are crispy, with no unpleasant tastes such as being old, astringent, or difficult to suck. Fresh food stores sell them all year round; however, ordinary small restaurants still do not have such dishes. People in the countryside find it difficult to afford them, as a small bowl of field frog food costs at least six or seven jiao. Sometimes, my parents would occasionally catch a small field frog in the rice field and stew a bowl of rice porridge for us children, which was truly a happy occasion.

Those who catch field frogs are professionals, mainly using the methods of fishing and digging burrows. Fishing is mostly done in the summer, but the results are limited, so few people do it. In the autumn and winter seasons, field frogs all hide in their burrows, making it a good time to search and catch them. A person skilled in catching can often catch dozens of them a day when they are lucky. However, these people are all old opium smokers who live from day to day, with no definite plans. There is a folk saying in my hometown: "Catch shrimp to buy opium, water comes and fire goes," which describes the lifestyle of these people.

To catch field frogs, you also need to know the secrets. First, you need to be able to tell what kind of mud burrow is a field frog burrow and what kind is a snake burrow. You cannot be mistaken. Then, you need to determine whether the field frog has left or is still hiding there before you start searching and catching. It is said that these methods can only be learned through apprenticeship. Field frog catchers also have knowledge that others do not have, which is that they can tell whether it will rain or be sunny based on the depth and complexity of the footprints of the field frog on the mud burrow entrance, and it always comes true. Therefore, they often become volunteer advisors to the old ladies in the countryside.

After spring comes, after the Awakening of Insects, the field frogs that have been hibernating in their burrows all leap into the rice fields. The field frog catchers then change their methods, carrying torches at night to the rice fields and seedling beds, squatting in a corner, extinguishing the torch, and slowly making a "ge ge ge" sound to lure the field frogs from afar. When you hear the sound of splashing water constantly coming from all around, quickly light the torch, and you can catch the field frogs one by one into the bamboo basket. After Grain Rain, it is said that the field frogs become very docile and will crouch on the ground and let people catch them when the torch shines on them. If it has rained during the day and the weather is erratic, the ground temperature suddenly rises, then it is very common to catch hundreds or thousands of them in a few minutes on a calm night.

There is also a very strange folk saying about the field frogs after Grain Rain. It is said that at this time, the field frogs often gather in ancient ponds or mountain streams, forming a tower of thousands of them, and at the bottom of the last field frog, there is always a very poisonous softshell turtle guarding there, so you cannot catch them all. However, there is no further information on whether anyone has encountered this.

The spring season is the peak period for the field frog market throughout the year. Because they have hibernated for a winter, their skin and meat are particularly tender, fresh, and fat, making them even more delicious. However, as far as I know, the production of field frogs near my hometown has long been very small. The local production is certainly not enough to supply the market, and the field frogs sold on the market now are all wholesale from the mountain counties around Shangyu, disguised as local field frogs for sale, and the meat tastes much inferior. However, they are still ten times better than those in Guangdong restaurants in Shanghai. I heard some time ago that someone planned to establish a farm specializing in raising field frogs. If it can be realized, it would be a very new and fresh business.

Family Letter

— Wei Yun

My father sent three letters from the countryside in a row, the last one being an express letter. My hometown, Zhijiao Town, is a small town in the countryside of Wanxian County. To get there, you have to go to Wanxian and then take a boat for a night; and the boat runs every three days. There is no post office in the town, and the delivery of letters is handled by a grocery store called Wanli, which brings them to Wanxian by boat every three days and mails them. Incoming letters are also handled in this way. However, they do not carry express letters or registered letters because they do not want to be responsible for things that require stamps. Therefore, to send an express letter from the town, you have to go to Wanxian in person to mail it, and if the boat schedule is not convenient, you have to stay overnight in Wanxian. That is the most troublesome thing. When I received the last pair of express letters, I thought something bad had happened at home, which is why they went to the trouble of sending express letters. However, the words in the letter were the same as in the previous two letters, except that the words "come back" were circled closely. The words in the letter were: My second brother is getting married, and my third brother is also getting married. You have been wandering outside for many years, and your father is very uneasy. It's not like we don't have food to eat at home, so come back. Next month is the third anniversary of your mother's death, and you should go to the grave to kowtow. Mentioning my deceased mother deeply moved me. Three months after my mother's death, my father married a young woman. In less than a year, my fourth younger brother was born, creating a deep divide between the family—especially between the brothers and our stepmother. I, as if I were an older sister to my stepmother, acted as the executioner of the family in front of my father, and ran away with the excuse of wanting to start a business. It has been two years since I left. After I left, my father seemed very regretful. He often asked my second and third brothers to write letters asking me to come back, but my second and third brothers clearly wrote that it was my father's intention. It's not that they didn't want me to come home, they told me that this family was even worse than before I left. My second sister-in-law could not bear the young mother's indirect scolding and had tried to commit suicide twice. My father had nothing to say about that matter, as if he had not heard or seen it. He forgot my mother's last words, which were to take good care of us three brothers. He was immersed in the arms of his young wife, and he forgot his responsibility as a father. In the express letter, he suddenly mentioned my mother's third anniversary, perhaps the old man was missing the virtuousness of his former wife in his heart. I cheered myself up and went home.

It was a rainy day. My father brought my second and third brothers to the boat pier to pick me up. We didn't speak on the way home. My father was just secretly looking at me, but he seemed very excited and was walking very fast as usual. Reaching Wanli Grocery Store, he said to my third brother, "I'll buy two catties of wine. You guys go home first." The wedding of my third brother was only three days away. There were many guests at home, all on my stepmother's side. I didn't greet them and went to my father's study to rest. Before it was time to light the lamp, my father called me from the living room and immediately came to the study. He happily patted me on the shoulder, casually flipped through my luggage, and ordered the servant to serve dinner in the study. The four of us, father and sons, silently drank wine under the light of a kerosene lamp. My second and third brothers deliberately asked about my situation outside, but my father never interrupted. He stopped his wine glass several times and quickly drank it dry again, seeming to have a very good alcohol tolerance.

That night I stayed in the study. My second and third brothers secretly came in a few times, but they didn't say much and left again.

The next morning, my second brother told me that my stepmother and father had argued for half the night last night. My father didn't seem to have slept, and he went out early in the morning with red eyes, saying that he was going to invite some relatives. I felt like I was dreaming and asked myself what I had come back for. My father is old. Can he withstand such stimulation? And I can't do what he imagined as a son.

Before noon, a woman's voice was scolding the servants in the corridor. The corridor was behind the study. My second brother stuck out his tongue at me and pointed at me with his little finger. But the scolding outside was very intense:

"Want to be a guest? Sleeping until the sun is shining on the roof ridge, what does that look like..."

A second, old voice answered, it was my father. He said, "The servant is lazy, what's the fuss about?" As he spoke, he stepped into the study with a bottle of wine in his hand, but he stopped at the door of the study for a long time without saying a word.

My second brother took the wine bottle from his hand, and the scolding outside was booming like thunder again.

Nonsense

— (Blow)

Japan's Hirota Koki formed a cabinet, and Britain expressed satisfaction. Old Man Tan said that Hirota advocates a policy of peace and does not advocate a scorched-earth policy, which seems better, but a scorched-earth policy is like cholera, and a peace policy is like tuberculosis. It seems better to outsiders, but the authorities are uncomfortable. Moreover, Hirota is under environmental pressure. How can we know that tuberculosis will not turn into cholera?

The US Navy discovered an international espionage case and found that valuable naval secret documents were stolen and sold to a certain foreign country. Old Man Tan said that the punks in our country, throwing coins, picking pockets, and stealing fountain pens, are their best tricks, but international thieves, stealing naval secret documents, the difference between big punks and small punks is really worlds apart. It is appropriate that those who steal hooks are condemned, while those who steal countries become princes.

Novel

Early Winter in Qingyang Port (13)

— Qiu Yuan

In the guest room, a gramophone and some records were found on the chairs. One by one, the records were played.——This one is very good, listen.——This one is even better! Look.——This "Diaen" is very nice to listen to.——The one before was masculine, but it's somewhat feminine, look, the name is so good, and the tone is so plaintive, DiaenMyDiaen.

Qiu Hua walked over, took her hand and embraced Zhuo Min's face, very forcefully, and gave Zhuo Min a very short kiss; Zhuo Min leaned back on the rattan chair, listening to the plaintive music. He also felt serene, and also felt the meaning and value of being a human. Days are always like this, so what else can he envy? However, what Zhuo Min felt was not only the taste of this short kiss, but rather the emotions beyond the kiss. Any woman would kiss him, but the reason why the taste of the same kiss is different is not only the kiss itself, such as the environment of the kiss, the time of the kiss, and the person of the kiss, but rather the emotions beyond the kiss. In others, besides the sensual feeling, what else is there? The same kiss, some is the enjoyment of the senses, and some is beyond the senses. What else is there besides the senses. If it is said that it is just a kiss, then it can be said that it is not worth half a penny. So when Qiu Zhou Hua kissed him, the serenity that Zhuo Min felt was not only sensual satisfaction, but rather like grasping a belief, a kind of spiritual detachment, and obtaining something greater and more sublime. These, only in Qiu Hua, can make him hunger for these emotions.

Women's Day Song

Drama

Thunder and Lightning Drama Society

Traffic (1300) 6 PM to 7 PM

Leader…Chen Yi

Nurse Ms. Wang……Chen Jie

Nurse Ms. Shen……Chen Xiang

Officer Zheng Ruibo……Lin Fei

Pregnant woman Zhu Wenhuan…Yu Wen

Dr. Zhang……Deng Qiong

Pastor Mao……Ma Xi

Traitor

Traitor is a realistic drama depicting social ugliness and cruelty; in Traitor there is a woman—Zhu Wenying—who struggles out of a feudal family and becomes a traitor.

In Traitor there is an officer—Ruibo—who becomes a traitor to feudal forces the first time, and a traitor to God the second time.

In Traitor there is a nurse—Ms. Shen—who specializes in flattering wealthy and powerful upper-class young mistresses, and who changes her attitude when they lose their money.

In Traitor there is a doctor—Dr. Zhang—who looks lustfully at young women and pretends to be attentive.

In Traitor there is an old pastor who wears a mask of benevolence and love for humanity, but is actually more ruthless than a wolf—Old Pastor.

In Traitor there is a nurse who colludes with evil—Ms. Wang.

Zhu Wenying and Zheng Ruibo reach the peak of love, and live together without getting married, thus becoming traitors to feudal forces.

In the necessary process of living together, Wenying is pregnant with a child. At this time, Ruibo is also a company commander in the army.

Wenying moves into the hospital because she is about to give birth. She lives in a second-class room, so the doctors and nurses in the hospital are very friendly to her. Nurse Ms. Shen becomes sisters with her, and Dr. Zhang considers her as his sister. She also recognizes an old pastor who is recuperating in the hospital as her father. In this way, she has a sister, a brother, and a father, so she is not lonely at all and lives a very happy life!

However, before the child in her womb is fully developed and able to come down, she begins to have bouts of intense stomach pain.

Suddenly, her husband Ruibo sneaks out to visit her when his army unit passes by here before heading to the front lines. Wenying is of course very happy, but later, because Ruibo only brought twenty yuan and could not pay the room fee and medical expenses, she is looked down upon by Ms. Shen. Dr. Zhang also feels embarrassed to lust after her because her man is here, so he takes a look at the thermometer and runs out! Wenying also confesses her and Ruibo's past to the old pastor, hoping that the old pastor will sympathize with them, but after hearing this, the old pastor puts on a stern face and does not even recognize her as his daughter! At this time, Wenying and Ruibo break the new idea of "there are still good people in the world" and more firmly confirm the old idea of "there are no good people in the world".

At this time, the army's bugle sounds! Because Ruibo sneaked out, he will be punished by military law if he does not go now, but he cannot bear to leave his wife who is rolling around in pain on the bed, and hesitates. The second bugle sounds again, but Wenying is in even more pain. Of course, he cannot leave so heartlessly, but in fact he has to leave!

Finally, Ruibo shoots the fetus in Wenying's womb, solving the problem and becoming a traitor to God.

At this time, Wenying will no longer have stomach pain! Ruibo does not have to leave his wife!

The old pastor sees this situation and takes out a police whistle, preparing to blow it. Ruibo snatches it away and puts it in Wenying's mouth, asking her to blow out her last breath from this silver whistle. Yes, Wenying's last breath is blown out from this silver whistle with a smile! The old pastor shouts out "These two traitors to God"!

At this time, the marching music of the army rushing to the front lines can be heard in the distance. The sound gradually decreases from loud to low, until it is faint and cannot be heard.

Storytelling with Stringed Instruments

Cai Xiaofang's Mao Family Book

Zhongxi (1040) 1:00 PM to 1:45 PM

Opening: "Spring Sorrow Song"

The slanting bridge leads to the courtyard, a piercing cold arises. Empty and silent, the embroidered chamber is warm with mandarin ducks. Reluctant to part, thoughts of spring reflect like a mirror. Dreamy shadows encroach, enough to dissolve the soul. Languidly, ill, she rises, too lazy to dress. Intoxicated, supporting her head, she cannot help but grow thin. Thinking of it, the lamp flower last night reported joy. But, the auspicious day is shallow and unclear. Pleasantly, the parrot is sincere, reciting poems haltingly. But, the swallow is foolishly persistent, complaining of hatred frequently. It is already, the twenty-four seasonal floral omens. Only the floating silk and chaotic catkins fill the gauze window. Once, I remember wandering the garden, treading every path. A kind of pity, engraved deep in the bones. Once, I remember, carefree, the library by the curtained hook was quiet. From the deep hall, the sound of playing chess was sent over. Once, I remember, the thirteen bejeweled columns of the zither were delicately plucked. Jade-like and round, truly the sound of white clouds. Once, I remember, the Pekingese puppy at the bottom of the screen spied with drunken eyes. A fairy awakening from the Yao Terrace, hairpin askew. That day, hurriedly covering my sleeves, the Yangguan Road. The horse slipped, the frost was thick, walking under the moon. Now, I wish to send the green, green riverside grass. To bring sorrow straight to the short and long pavilion. Only getting by, the sewing bees and butterflies are bored and helpless. Secretly buying rouge, embracing fallen petals. Therefore, my gaze cuts off the green mist and water by the bridge. North of the Magnolia Hall, I tread on the remaining spring. Blaming Eastern Emperor for being too troublesome.

Movies

Star's New Film Casts

In "Lovers in Exile" and "Peach Blossoms After the Robbery," Hong Shen expressed his sorrow for the rise and fall of his homeland. Now, his new work "Lovers in Exile" has been completely written. Undoubtedly, this is another profoundly meaningful social drama. It has been decided that Zhang Shichuan will direct it, and the start of filming will not be far off.

"New and Old Shanghai" Cheng Bugao is continuing with "Brothers' Line" and preparing to film the new work, also written by Hong Shen, "New and Old Shanghai." This is a satirical and humorous comedy. The light and dark sides of the metropolis are clearly reflected on the screen. The explanation of the plot has already begun the day before yesterday. The actors include Wang Xianqi, Shu Xiuwen, Xie Yunqing, and others.

"King Kong Mine" and "Jade Horse" are where Xu Xinfu opened up a new path in the domestic film industry, giving the audience a new taste. In this regard, we are hoping for more of his efforts. Now, his new work "King Kong Mine" is about to be prepared for filming. This is a work standing on the same road as "Jade Horse." For eager audiences, this should be news worth introducing to you.

In addition, Mr. Ouyang Yuqian also has two or three new scripts completed, and Mr. Liu Na'ou has also completed one. In the near future, they can all be filmed separately.

Dance Market Published Today

The small semi-monthly magazine "Dance Market," which has been prepared for a long time by Modern Publishing House, was published today. The book is in two sections, the other side is "Modern Women." The content includes twenty articles, about the dynamics of modern women and the secrets and scandals of the dance world. Everything is realistic. There are more than twenty copperplate illustrations, all of which are valuable photographs of modern women and dance stars. The book has sixty-four pages and is finely printed on cream-colored Dowling paper. Each copy sells for one dime. If you need a sample, you can attach seven cents in postage and send it to Modern Publishing House, 77 Ruikang Lane, Dithwell Road, Shanghai, and it will be sent to you immediately. Subscribers for the whole year will also receive a signed art photo of the cover girl, Miss Wang Xueqin.

Star's New Film "Flowers of Spring" Three Leads

Yan Yuexian Gao Zhanfei Sun Min

Silver Scribbles

— Zhizhi

"It is said that 'Philosopher' is not a pseudonym for Xu Suling. This is indeed very interesting. 'Certain people often use pseudonyms to praise themselves and deceive the masses,'" that is a common trick, which need not be said again; however, those who are "actively working" and have produced "a little" achievement are not Zhiyu, so what is Zhiyu "praising himself" for? What is "praised" is only the likes of Mr. Philosopher.

I remember we said before that Shu Xiuwen and Pan Zinong were separated, but soon after, another "hero" jumped out and said that this was a rumor with provocative intentions. The reason was that he was very familiar with "my husband" (forgive me for quoting the "old-fashioned" term again), and according to him, "husband and wife" were very harmonious.

Now, the fact that Shu and Pan are separated has gradually been confirmed. Where has that "hero" gone? I do not know. Probably he has transformed into another face, right?

What has been done cannot be hidden. "Heroes!"

Mr. Philosopher has probably become "indulgent" because of "humility." To see the "original form" of the "heroes," "indulgence" is better than "humility," because when demons transform into beautiful women, they have to be a little "humble," but when they can't help but become "indulgent," that is already the revealing of their original form. Although the original form appears hideous and terrifying, it makes the audience shrink back at first sight, preventing them from being deceived again. That point is, in any case, beneficial to the audience.
